```ts
   1 | import type { AnyColumn } from "drizzle-orm";
   2 | import { sql } from "drizzle-orm";
   3 | import { pgTableCreator, text, timestamp } from "drizzle-orm/pg-core";
   4 | 
   5 | import type { DbPrescribedItem } from "./schema/types";
   6 | import type { AdherenceItem, PrescriptionWithItems } from "./zod";
   7 | 
   8 | type AdherenceRecommendation = {
   9 | 	action: string;
  10 | 	message: string;
  11 | 	type: "adherence" | "positive";
  12 | };
  13 | 
  14 | type AdherenceDataPoint = {
  15 | 	adherenceRate: number;
  16 | 	drugId: string;
  17 | };
  18 | 
  19 | export function parseFrequency(frequency: string): number {
  20 | 	// Parse frequency string (e.g., "BID" = 2, "TID" = 3, "QD" = 1, "Q4H" = 6)
  21 | 	const frequencyMap: Record<string, number> = {
  22 | 		QD: 1,
  23 | 		BID: 2,
  24 | 		TID: 3,
  25 | 		QID: 4,
  26 | 		Q4H: 6,
  27 | 		Q6H: 4,
  28 | 		Q8H: 3,
  29 | 		Q12H: 2,
  30 | 		PRN: 2
  31 | 	};
  32 | 	return frequencyMap[frequency.toUpperCase()] ?? 2;
  33 | }
  34 | export function getAdherenceStatus(rate: number): string {
  35 | 	if (rate >= 80) return "good";
  36 | 	if (rate >= 50) return "moderate";
  37 | 	return "poor";
  38 | }
  39 | 
  40 | export function generateAdherenceRecommendations(adherenceData: AdherenceDataPoint[]) {
  41 | 	const recommendations: AdherenceRecommendation[] = [];
  42 | 	const poorAdherence = adherenceData.filter(d => d.adherenceRate < 50);
  43 | 
  44 | 	if (poorAdherence.length > 0) {
  45 | 		recommendations.push({
  46 | 			type: "adherence",
  47 | 			message: `Poor adherence detected for ${poorAdherence.length} medication(s)`,
  48 | 			action: "Schedule medication counseling session"
  49 | 		});
  50 | 	}
  51 | 
  52 | 	const highAdherence = adherenceData.filter(d => d.adherenceRate >= 80);
  53 | 	if (highAdherence.length > 0) {
  54 | 		recommendations.push({
  55 | 			type: "positive",
  56 | 			message: `Good adherence for ${highAdherence.length} medication(s)`,
  57 | 			action: "Continue current regimen"
  58 | 		});
  59 | 	}
  60 | 
  61 | 	return recommendations;
  62 | }
  63 | 
  64 | export function groupByMonth(prescriptions: PrescriptionWithItems[]) {
  65 | 	const monthMap = new Map();
  66 | 
  67 | 	for (const prescription of prescriptions) {
  68 | 		const month = prescription.issuedDate.toISOString().slice(0, 7);
  69 | 		if (!monthMap.has(month)) {
  70 | 			monthMap.set(month, {
  71 | 				month,
  72 | 				prescriptionCount: 0,
  73 | 				totalItems: 0
  74 | 			});
  75 | 		}
  76 | 
  77 | 		const stats = monthMap.get(month);
  78 | 		stats.prescriptionCount++;
  79 | 		stats.totalItems += prescription.prescribedItems.length;
  80 | 	}
  81 | 
  82 | 	return Array.from(monthMap.entries())
  83 | 		.map(([_, stats]) => stats)
  84 | 		.sort((a, b) => a.month.localeCompare(b.month));
  85 | }
  86 | 
  87 | export function calculateDaysSupply(item: DbPrescribedItem): number {
  88 | 	const quantity = item.dosageValue || 0;
  89 | 	const dosagePerDay = (item.dosageValue || 0) * parseFrequency(item.frequency);
  90 | 	return dosagePerDay > 0 ? Math.floor(quantity / dosagePerDay) : 0;
  91 | }
  92 | 
  93 | export function calculateRefillInterval(item: DbPrescribedItem): number {
  94 | 	// Calculate when next refill is due (typically 80% of days supply)
  95 | 	const daysSupply = calculateDaysSupply(item);
  96 | 	return Math.floor(daysSupply * 0.8);
  97 | }
  98 | 
  99 | type DoctorStats = {
 100 | 	doctorName: string | undefined;
 101 | 	prescriptionCount: number;
 102 | 	uniquePatients: Set<string>;
 103 | 	totalItems: number;
 104 | };
 105 | 
 106 | export function groupByDoctor(
 107 | 	prescriptions: (PrescriptionWithItems & {
 108 | 		doctor?: { name: string } | null;
 109 | 	})[]
 110 | ) {
 111 | 	const doctorMap = new Map<string, DoctorStats>();
 112 | 
 113 | 	for (const prescription of prescriptions) {
 114 | 		const doctorId = prescription.doctorId;
 115 | 		if (!doctorMap.has(doctorId ?? "")) {
 116 | 			doctorMap.set(doctorId ?? "", {
 117 | 				doctorName: prescription.doctor?.name,
 118 | 				prescriptionCount: 0,
 119 | 				uniquePatients: new Set(),
 120 | 				totalItems: 0
 121 | 			});
 122 | 		}
 123 | 
 124 | 		const stats = doctorMap.get(doctorId ?? "");
 125 | 		if (!stats) continue;
 126 | 		stats.prescriptionCount++;
 127 | 		stats.uniquePatients.add(prescription.patientId);
 128 | 		stats.totalItems += prescription.prescribedItems.length;
 129 | 	}
 130 | 
 131 | 	return Array.from(doctorMap.entries()).map(([id, stats]) => {
 132 | 		return {
 133 | 			doctorId: id,
 134 | 			...stats,
 135 | 			uniquePatients: stats.uniquePatients.size
 136 | 		};
 137 | 	});
 138 | }
 139 | 
 140 | export function groupByDrug(prescriptions: PrescriptionWithItems[]) {
 141 | 	const drugMap = new Map<
 142 | 		string,
 143 | 		{
 144 | 			drugName: string | undefined;
 145 | 			prescriptionCount: number;
 146 | 			totalDoses: number;
 147 | 			totalQuantity: number;
 148 | 		}
 149 | 	>();
 150 | 
 151 | 	for (const prescription of prescriptions) {
 152 | 		for (const item of prescription.prescribedItems) {
 153 | 			const drugId = item.drugId;
 154 | 			if (!drugMap.has(drugId)) {
 155 | 				drugMap.set(drugId, {
 156 | 					drugName: item.drug?.name,
 157 | 					prescriptionCount: 0,
 158 | 					totalDoses: 0,
 159 | 					totalQuantity: 0
 160 | 				});
 161 | 			}
 162 | 
 163 | 			const stats = drugMap.get(drugId);
 164 | 			if (!stats) continue;
 165 | 			stats.prescriptionCount++;
 166 | 			stats.totalDoses += item.dosageValue || 0;
 167 | 			// Note: prescribedItem doesn't have a 'quantity' field, using dosageValue as total quantity
 168 | 			stats.totalQuantity += item.dosageValue || 0;
 169 | 		}
 170 | 	}
 171 | 
 172 | 	return Array.from(drugMap.entries())
 173 | 		.map(([id, stats]) => {
 174 | 			return {
 175 | 				drugId: id,
 176 | 				...stats
 177 | 			};
 178 | 		})
 179 | 		.sort((a, b) => b.prescriptionCount - a.prescriptionCount);
 180 | }

 206 | export function takeFirstOrNull<TData>(data: Array<TData>) {

 208 | }
 209 | 
 210 | export function takeFirstOrThrow<TData>(data: Array<TData>, errorMessage?: string) {
 211 | 	const first = takeFirstOrNull(data);
 212 | 
 213 | 	if (!first) {
 214 | 		throw new Error(errorMessage ?? "Item not found");
 215 | 	}
 216 | 
 217 | 	return first;
 218 | }

 220 | export function isEmpty<TColumn extends AnyColumn>(column: TColumn) {
 221 | 	return sql<boolean>`
 222 |     case
 223 |       when ${column} is null then true
 224 |       when ${column} = '' then true
 225 |       when ${column}::text = '[]' then true
 226 |       when ${column}::text = '{}' then true
 227 |       else false
 228 |     end
 229 |   `;
 230 | }

 232 | /**
 233 |  * Converts camelCase to snake_case
 234 |  * @param str - The camelCase string to convert
 235 |  * @returns The snake_case version of the string
 236 |  */
 237 | function toSnakeCase(str: string): string {
 238 | 	return str.replace(/[A-Z]/g, letter => `_${letter.toLowerCase()}`);
 239 | }
 240 | 
 241 | /**
 242 |  * Creates a key-value for file upload columns
 243 |  * @param columnPrefix - The prefix for the column names in camelCase (e.g., 'offeringDocument', 'profilePicture')
 244 |  * @returns Object with only url column
 245 |  */
 246 | export function createFileUrlColumn<T extends string>(columnPrefix: T) {
 247 | 	const snakeCase = toSnakeCase(columnPrefix);
 248 | 	return {
 249 | 		[`${columnPrefix}Url`]: text(`${snakeCase}_url`)
 250 | 	} as Record<`${T}Url`, ReturnType<typeof text>>;
 251 | }
 252 | 
 253 | /**
 254 |  * Creates a key-value for NOT NULL file upload columns
 255 |  * @param columnPrefix - The prefix for the column names in camelCase (e.g., 'offeringDocument', 'profilePicture')
 256 |  * @returns Object with only NOT NULL url column
 257 |  */
 258 | export function createRequiredFileUrlColumn<T extends string>(columnPrefix: T) {
 259 | 	const snakeCase = toSnakeCase(columnPrefix);
 260 | 	return {
 261 | 		[`${columnPrefix}Url`]: text(`${snakeCase}_url`).notNull()
 262 | 	} as Record<`${T}Url`, ReturnType<ReturnType<typeof text>["notNull"]>>;
 263 | }
 264 | 
 265 | /**
 266 |  * Creates a pair of columns for file uploads (fileName and url)
 267 |  * @param columnPrefix - The prefix for the column names in camelCase (e.g., 'offeringDocument', 'profilePicture')
 268 |  * @returns Object with fileName and url columns
 269 |  */
 270 | export function createFileColumns<T extends string>(columnPrefix: T) {
 271 | 	const snakeCase = toSnakeCase(columnPrefix);
 272 | 	return {
 273 | 		[`${columnPrefix}FileName`]: text(`${snakeCase}_file_name`),
 274 | 		[`${columnPrefix}Url`]: text(`${snakeCase}_url`)
 275 | 	} as Record<`${T}FileName` | `${T}Url`, ReturnType<typeof text>>;
 276 | }

 280 |  * @returns Object with NOT NULL fileName and url columns
 281 |  */
 282 | export function createRequiredFileColumns<T extends string>(columnPrefix: T) {
 283 | 	const snakeCase = toSnakeCase(columnPrefix);
 284 | 	return {
 285 | 		[`${columnPrefix}FileName`]: text(`${snakeCase}_file_name`).notNull(),
 286 | 		[`${columnPrefix}Url`]: text(`${snakeCase}_url`).notNull()
 287 | 	} as Record<`${T}FileName` | `${T}Url`, ReturnType<ReturnType<typeof text>["notNull"]>>;
 288 | }
 289 | 
 290 | // Helper functions
 291 | export function calculateAdherenceMetrics(prescribedItems: AdherenceItem[]) {
 292 | 	let totalAdherence = 0;
 293 | 	let count = 0;
 294 | 
 295 | 	for (const item of prescribedItems) {
 296 | 		const expectedDoses = calculateExpectedDoses(
 297 | 			item,
 298 | 			item.prescription?.issuedDate ?? new Date(),
 299 | 			item.prescription?.validUntil ?? new Date()
 300 | 		);
 301 | 		const dispensedDoses =
 302 | 			item.dispenses?.reduce(
 303 | 				(sum: number, dispense: { quantityDispensed: number }) =>
 304 | 					sum + dispense.quantityDispensed / (item.dosageValue || 1),
 305 | 				0
 306 | 			) ?? 0;
 307 | 
 308 | 		const adherence = expectedDoses > 0 ? (dispensedDoses / expectedDoses) * 100 : 0;
 309 | 		totalAdherence += adherence;
 310 | 		count++;
 311 | 	}
 312 | 
 313 | 	return {
 314 | 		overallAdherence: count > 0 ? totalAdherence / count : 0,
 315 | 		status: getAdherenceStatus(totalAdherence / count)
 316 | 	};
 317 | }
 318 | 
 319 | export function calculateExpectedDoses(item: AdherenceItem, startDate: Date, endDate: Date) {
 320 | 	const days = Math.ceil((endDate.getTime() - startDate.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 321 | 	const frequencyPerDay = parseFrequency(item.frequency);
 322 | 	return days * frequencyPerDay * (item.dosageValue || 1);
 323 | }
 324 | 
 325 | /**
 326 |  * Standardized Database Result Wrapper
 327 |  */
 328 | export async function safeDbQuery<T>(queryFn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<{ data: T | null; error: string | null }> {
 329 | 	try {
 330 | 		const result = await queryFn();
 331 | 		return { data: result, error: null };
 332 | 	} catch (err) {
 333 | 		console.error("[DATABASE_ERROR]:", err);
 334 | 		return {
 335 | 			data: null,
 336 | 			error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : "An unexpected database error occurred"
 337 | 		};
 338 | 	}
 339 | }
```

```ts
   1 | import path from "node:path";
   2 | import { sql } from "drizzle-orm";
   3 | import { drizzle } from "drizzle-orm/node-postgres";
   4 | import { migrate } from "drizzle-orm/node-postgres/migrator"; // Updated import
   5 | import { Pool } from "pg";
   6 | import { relations } from "./schema/relations";
   7 | 
   8 | if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) {
   9 | 	throw new Error("DATABASE_URL is not set");
  10 | }
  11 | const globalForDb = globalThis as unknown as {
  12 | 	pool: Pool | undefined;
  13 | };
  14 | 
  15 | // Simple Logger Helper
  16 | const logger = {
  17 | 	info: (msg: string, ...args: unknown[]) => console.log(`[DB-INFO] ${msg}`, ...args),
  18 | 	warn: (msg: string, ...args: unknown[]) => console.warn(`[DB-WARN] ${msg}`, ...args),
  19 | 	error: (msg: string, ...args: unknown[]) => console.error(`[DB-ERROR] ${msg}`, ...args),
  20 | 	debug: (msg: string, ...args: unknown[]) =>
  21 | 		process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production" && console.debug(`[DB-DEBUG] ${msg}`, ...args)
  22 | };
  23 | 
  24 | // Use pg Pool instead of postgres.js
  25 | const pool =
  26 | 	globalForDb.pool ??
  27 | 	new Pool({
  28 | 		connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL,
  29 | 		max: 10,
  30 | 		idleTimeoutMillis: 20000,
  31 | 		connectionTimeoutMillis: 10000
  32 | 	});
  33 | 
  34 | if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") globalForDb.pool = pool;
  35 | 
  36 | export const db = drizzle({
  37 | 	client: pool,
  38 | 	// Note: relations are passed via the schema object in the new Drizzle API
  39 | 	relations,
  40 | 	logger: process.env.NODE_ENV === "development"
  41 | });
  42 | 
  43 | export function createDb() {
  44 | 	return drizzle({
  45 | 		client: new Pool({ connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL }),
  46 | 		relations
  47 | 	});
  48 | }
  49 | 
  50 | // export const db = drizzle(pool, { schema });
  51 | 
  52 | export async function checkIsDbReady(): Promise<boolean> {
  53 | 	try {
  54 | 		await db.execute(sql`SELECT 1`);
  55 | 		logger.debug("Database connection check successful");
  56 | 		return true;
  57 | 	} catch (error) {
  58 | 		logger.error("Database connection check failed", error);
  59 | 		return false;
  60 | 	}
  61 | }
  62 | 
  63 | let migrationFnCalled = false;
  64 | 
  65 | export async function runMigrations(): Promise<void> {
  66 | 	const fnName = "runMigrations";
  67 | 
  68 | 	if (migrationFnCalled) {
  69 | 		logger.debug(`[${fnName}] Skipping migration (already called)`);
  70 | 		return;
  71 | 	}
  72 | 
  73 | 	migrationFnCalled = true;
  74 | 
  75 | 	if (process.env.IS_BUILD) {
  76 | 		logger.info(`[${fnName}] Skipping migrations during build process (NODE_ENV: ${process.env.NODE_ENV})`);
  77 | 		return;
  78 | 	}
  79 | 
  80 | 	// Note: Usually you WANT to run migrations in production.
  81 | 	// If you strictly want to skip them, keep this, but ensure your CI/CD handles it.
  82 | 	if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
  83 | 		logger.info(`[${fnName}] Running in ${process.env.NODE_ENV}, applying migrations...`);
  84 | 	} else {
  85 | 		logger.info(`[${fnName}] Applying migrations for production...`);
  86 | 	}
  87 | 
  88 | 	const migrationsFolder = path.join(process.cwd(), "packages/db/src/migrations");
  89 | 
  90 | 	try {
  91 | 		logger.info(`[${fnName}] Starting migration process...`);
  92 | 		await migrate(db, { migrationsFolder });
  93 | 		logger.info(`[${fnName}] ✅ Database migration completed successfully`);
  94 | 	} catch (error) {
  95 | 		logger.error(`[${fnName}] ❌ Database migration failed`, error);
  96 | 		throw error;
  97 | 	}
  98 | }
  99 | 
 100 | export type DB = typeof db;
 101 | export type DBType = Parameters<Parameters<typeof db.transaction>[0]>[0];
 102 | export type DBorTx = DB | DBType;
```

`reset.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import "dotenv/config";
   2 | import { stdin as input, stdout as output } from "node:process";
   3 | import * as readline from "node:readline";
   4 | import { Client } from "pg"; // Updated import
   5 | 
   6 | const DATABASE_URL = process.env.DATABASE_URL;
   7 | 
   8 | if (!DATABASE_URL) {
   9 | 	console.error("❌ DATABASE_URL environment variable is not set");
  10 | 	process.exit(1);
  11 | }
  12 | 
  13 | async function askConfirmation(): Promise<boolean> {
  14 | 	const args = process.argv.slice(2);
  15 | 	if (args.includes("--force") || args.includes("-y")) {
  16 | 		return true;
  17 | 	}
  18 | 
  19 | 	const rl = readline.createInterface({ input, output });
  20 | 	try {
  21 | 		const answer = await new Promise<string>(resolve => {
  22 | 			rl.question("\n⚠️  WARNING: This will delete ALL data in the public schema. Continue? (y/N): ", resolve);
  23 | 		});
  24 | 		return answer.toLowerCase() === "y" || answer.toLowerCase() === "yes";
  25 | 	} finally {
  26 | 		rl.close();
  27 | 	}
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | async function resetDatabase() {
  31 | 	const confirmed = await askConfirmation();
  32 | 	if (!confirmed) {
  33 | 		console.log("❌ Reset cancelled.");
  34 | 		return;
  35 | 	}
  36 | 
  37 | 	console.log("\n🧹 Preparing to reset PostgreSQL database...");
  38 | 	const maskedUrl = DATABASE_URL?.replace(/:([^:@]+)@/, ":****@");
  39 | 	console.log(`📡 Connecting to: ${maskedUrl}`);
  40 | 
  41 | 	// Initialize the pg Client
  42 | 	const client = new Client({ connectionString: DATABASE_URL });
  43 | 
  44 | 	try {
  45 | 		await client.connect();
  46 | 		console.log("✅ Database connection successful\n");
  47 | 
  48 | 		console.log("🔥 Dropping and recreating public schema...");
  49 | 
  50 | 		// pg uses "BEGIN", "COMMIT", "ROLLBACK" for transactions
  51 | 		await client.query("BEGIN");
  52 | 		try {
  53 | 			await client.query("DROP SCHEMA IF EXISTS public CASCADE");
  54 | 			await client.query("CREATE SCHEMA public");
  55 | 			await client.query("GRANT ALL ON SCHEMA public TO public");
  56 | 			await client.query("COMMENT ON SCHEMA public IS 'standard public schema'");
  57 | 			await client.query("COMMIT");
  58 | 		} catch (e) {
  59 | 			await client.query("ROLLBACK");
  60 | 			throw e;
  61 | 		}
  62 | 
  63 | 		console.log("✅ Schema reset successful.");
  64 | 		console.log("\n✨ Database reset complete!");
  65 | 		console.log("\n🚀 Next steps:");
  66 | 		console.log("   1. Run migrations: bun run db:migrate");
  67 | 		console.log("   2. Seed database: bun run db:seed");
  68 | 		console.log("   3. Start the app: bun run dev");
  69 | 	} catch (error) {
  70 | 		console.error("\n❌ Reset failed:", error instanceof Error ? error.message : error);
  71 | 		process.exit(1);
  72 | 	} finally {
  73 | 		await client.end();
  74 | 	}
  75 | }
  76 | 
  77 | resetDatabase();
```

`schema/index.ts`:

```ts
   1 | export * from "./auth";
```

`schema/relations.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { defineRelations } from "drizzle-orm";
   2 | 
   3 | import * as schema from "../schema";
   4 | 
   5 | export const relations = defineRelations(schema, r => ({
   6 | 	user: {
   7 | 		sessions: r.many.session(),
   8 | 		accounts: r.many.account(),
   9 | 		clinic: r.one.clinic({
  10 | 			from: r.user.clinicId,
  11 | 			to: r.clinic.id
  12 | 		}),
  13 | 		files: r.many.file({
  14 | 			from: r.user.id,
  15 | 			to: r.file.userId
  16 | 		}),
  17 | 		folders: r.many.folder({
  18 | 			from: r.user.id,
  19 | 			to: r.folder.userId
  20 | 		}),
  21 | 		twoFactors: r.many.twoFactor({
  22 | 			from: r.user.id,
  23 | 			to: r.twoFactor.userId
  24 | 		}),
  25 | 		quota: r.one.userQuota({
  26 | 			from: r.user.id,
  27 | 			to: r.userQuota.userId
  28 | 		}),
  29 | 		clinics: r.many.clinicMember({
  30 | 			from: r.user.id,
  31 | 			to: r.clinicMember.userId
  32 | 		}),
  33 | 		doctors: r.many.doctor({
  34 | 			from: r.user.id,
  35 | 			to: r.doctor.userId
  36 | 		}),
  37 | 		staffs: r.many.staff({
  38 | 			from: r.user.id,
  39 | 			to: r.staff.userId
  40 | 		}),
  41 | 		patients: r.many.patient({
  42 | 			from: r.user.id,
  43 | 			to: r.patient.userId,
  44 | 			alias: "PatientUser"
  45 | 		}),
  46 | 		createdPatients: r.many.patient({
  47 | 			from: r.user.id,
  48 | 			to: r.patient.createdById,
  49 | 			alias: "PatientCreatedBy"
  50 | 		}),
  51 | 		guardians: r.many.guardian({
  52 | 			from: r.user.id,
  53 | 			to: r.guardian.userId
  54 | 		}),
  55 | 		createdMedicalRecord: r.many.medicalRecord({
  56 | 			from: r.user.id,
  57 | 			to: r.medicalRecord.doctorId,
  58 | 			alias: "createdBy"
  59 | 		}),
  60 | 		notifications: r.many.notification({
  61 | 			from: r.user.id,
  62 | 			to: r.notification.userId
  63 | 		}),
  64 | 		invitesCreated: r.many.invite({
  65 | 			from: r.user.id,
  66 | 			to: r.invite.createdBy,
  67 | 			alias: "createdBy"
  68 | 		}),
  69 | 		invitesUsed: r.many.invite({
  70 | 			from: r.user.id,
  71 | 			to: r.invite.usedBy,
  72 | 			alias: "usedBy"
  73 | 		}),
  74 | 		twoFactor: r.one.twoFactor({
  75 | 			from: r.user.id,
  76 | 			to: r.twoFactor.userId
  77 | 		}),
  78 | 		clinicMemberships: r.many.clinicMember({
  79 | 			from: r.user.id,
  80 | 			to: r.clinicMember.userId
  81 | 		}),
  82 | 		doctorProfile: r.one.doctor({
  83 | 			from: r.user.id,
  84 | 			to: r.doctor.userId
  85 | 		}),
  86 | 		staffProfile: r.one.staff({
  87 | 			from: r.user.id,
  88 | 			to: r.staff.userId
  89 | 		}),
  90 | 		patientProfile: r.one.patient({
  91 | 			from: r.user.id,
  92 | 			to: r.patient.userId,
  93 | 			alias: "PatientUser"
  94 | 		}),
  95 | 		patientsCreated: r.many.patient({
  96 | 			from: r.user.id,
  97 | 			to: r.patient.createdById,
  98 | 			alias: "PatientCreatedBy"
  99 | 		}),
 100 | 		guardianRelations: r.many.guardian({
 101 | 			from: r.user.id,
 102 | 			to: r.guardian.userId
 103 | 		})
 104 | 	},
 105 | 
 106 | 	// Account relations
 107 | 	accounts: {
 108 | 		user: r.one.user({
 109 | 			from: r.account.userId,
 110 | 			to: r.user.id
 111 | 		})
 112 | 	},
 113 | 
 114 | 	// Session relations
 115 | 	sessions: {
 116 | 		user: r.one.user({
 117 | 			from: r.session.userId,
 118 | 			to: r.user.id
 119 | 		})
 120 | 	},
 121 | 
 122 | 	// Notification relations
 123 | 	notifications: {
 124 | 		user: r.one.user({
 125 | 			from: r.notification.userId,
 126 | 			to: r.user.id
 127 | 		}),
 128 | 		clinic: r.one.clinic({
 129 | 			from: r.notification.clinicId,
 130 | 			to: r.clinic.id
 131 | 		})
 132 | 	},
 133 | 
 134 | 	// Folder relations (self-referential)
 135 | 	folders: {
 136 | 		user: r.one.user({
 137 | 			from: r.folder.userId,
 138 | 			to: r.user.id
 139 | 		}),
 140 | 		parent: r.one.folder({
 141 | 			from: r.folder.parentId,
 142 | 			to: r.folder.id,
 143 | 			alias: "subfolders"
 144 | 		}),
 145 | 		subfolders: r.many.folder({
 146 | 			from: r.folder.id,
 147 | 			to: r.folder.parentId,
 148 | 			alias: "subfolders"
 149 | 		}),
 150 | 		files: r.many.file({
 151 | 			from: r.folder.id,
 152 | 			to: r.file.folderId
 153 | 		})
 154 | 	},
 155 | 
 156 | 	// File relations
 157 | 	files: {
 158 | 		user: r.one.user({
 159 | 			from: r.file.userId,

 797 | 	},
 798 | 	session: {
 799 | 		user: r.one.user({
 800 | 			from: r.session.userId,
 801 | 			to: r.user.id
 802 | 		})
 803 | 	},
 804 | 	account: {
 805 | 		user: r.one.user({
 806 | 			from: r.account.userId,
 807 | 			to: r.user.id
 808 | 		})
 809 | 	},
 810 | 
 811 | 	vaccineInventory: {
 812 | 		clinic: r.one.clinic({
 813 | 			from: r.vaccineInventory.clinicId,
 814 | 			to: r.clinic.id
 815 | 		}),
 816 | 		immunizations: r.many.immunization({
 817 | 			from: r.vaccineInventory.id,
 818 | 			to: r.immunization.vaccineInventoryId
 819 | 		})
 820 | 	},
 821 | 
 822 | 	aiReport: {
 823 | 		patient: r.one.patient({
 824 | 			from: r.aiReport.patientId,
 825 | 			to: r.patient.id
 826 | 		}),
 827 | 		doctor: r.one.doctor({
 828 | 			from: r.aiReport.doctorId,
 829 | 			to: r.doctor.id
 830 | 		}),
 831 | 		clinic: r.one.clinic({
 832 | 			from: r.aiReport.clinicId,
 833 | 			to: r.clinic.id
 834 | 		}),
 835 | 		generator: r.one.user({
 836 | 			from: r.aiReport.generatedBy,
 837 | 			to: r.user.id
 838 | 		})
 839 | 	}
 840 | }));

```
`schema/shop.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { integer, numeric, pgEnum, pgTable, text, timestamp, uuid, varchar } from "drizzle-orm/pg-core";
   2 | import { user } from "./auth";
   3 | 
   4 | const badgeValues = ["New", "Sale", "Featured", "Limited"] as const;
   5 | const inventoryValues = ["in-stock", "backorder", "preorder"] as const;
   6 | 
   7 | export const badgeEnum = pgEnum("badge", badgeValues);
   8 | export const inventoryEnum = pgEnum("inventory", inventoryValues);
   9 | 
  10 | export const products = pgTable("products", {
  11 | 	id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  12 | 	name: varchar("name", { length: 256 }).notNull(),
  13 | 	description: text("description").notNull(),
  14 | 	price: numeric("price", { precision: 10, scale: 2 }).notNull(),
  15 | 	badge: badgeEnum("badge"),
  16 | 	rating: numeric("rating", { precision: 3, scale: 2 }).notNull().default("0"),
  17 | 	reviews: integer("reviews").notNull().default(0),
  18 | 	image: varchar("image", { length: 512 }).notNull(),
  19 | 	inventory: inventoryEnum("inventory").notNull().default("in-stock"),
  20 | 	createdAt: timestamp("created_at").defaultNow().notNull()
  21 | });
  22 | 
  23 | export type ProductSelect = typeof products.$inferSelect;
  24 | export type ProductInsert = typeof products.$inferInsert;
  25 | 
  26 | // Cart items table - stores items in user's cart
  27 | export const cartItems = pgTable("cart_items", {
  28 | 	id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  29 | 	productId: uuid("product_id")
  30 | 		.notNull()
  31 | 		.references(() => products.id, { onDelete: "cascade" }),
  32 | 	quantity: integer("quantity").notNull().default(1),
  33 | 	createdAt: timestamp("created_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
  34 | 	updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at").defaultNow().notNull()
  35 | });
  36 | 
  37 | export type CartItemSelect = typeof cartItems.$inferSelect & typeof products.$inferSelect;
  38 | 
  39 | export type CartItemInsert = typeof cartItems.$inferInsert;
  40 | 
  41 | // Export enum value types inferred from the enum definitions
  42 | export type BadgeValue = (typeof badgeValues)[number];
  43 | export type InventoryValue = (typeof inventoryValues)[number];
  44 | 
  45 | const orderStatusValues = ["pending", "paid", "failed"] as const;
  46 | export const orderStatusEnum = pgEnum("order_status", orderStatusValues);
  47 | 
  48 | export const orders = pgTable("orders", {
  49 | 	id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  50 | 	userId: text("user_id")
  51 | 		.notNull()
  52 | 		.references(() => user.id, { onDelete: "cascade" }),
  53 | 	stripeSessionId: text("stripe_session_id"),
  54 | 	status: orderStatusEnum("status").notNull().default("pending"),
  55 | 	total: numeric("total", { precision: 10, scale: 2 }).notNull(),
  56 | 	createdAt: timestamp("created_at").defaultNow().notNull()
  57 | });
  58 | 
  59 | export const orderItems = pgTable("order_items", {
  60 | 	id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  61 | 	orderId: uuid("order_id")
  62 | 		.notNull()
  63 | 		.references(() => orders.id, { onDelete: "cascade" }),
  64 | 	productId: uuid("product_id").references(() => products.id, {
  65 | 		onDelete: "set null"
  66 | 	}),
  67 | 	name: varchar("name", { length: 256 }).notNull(),
  68 | 	price: numeric("price", { precision: 10, scale: 2 }).notNull(),
  69 | 	quantity: integer("quantity").notNull(),
  70 | 	image: varchar("image", { length: 512 }).notNull()
  71 | });
  72 | 
  73 | export type OrderSelect = typeof orders.$inferSelect;
  74 | export type OrderInsert = typeof orders.$inferInsert;
  75 | export type OrderItemSelect = typeof orderItems.$inferSelect;
  76 | export type OrderItemInsert = typeof orderItems.$inferInsert;
```

`seed.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // t3 env reads import.meta.env; seed scripts run
   2 | import dotenv from "dotenv";
   3 | 
   4 | import type { DB } from "./";
   5 | import { runSeed } from "./seed/seed";
   6 | import drugSeed from "./seed/seed-drugs";
   7 | import wfaSeed from "./seed/seed-wfa";
   8 | 
   9 | dotenv.config({
  10 | 	path: "../../apps/web/.env"
  11 | });
  12 | 
  13 | /**
  14 |  * Master seed runner
  15 |  */
  16 | async function runAllSeeds(db: DB) {
  17 | 	console.log("🚀 Starting Master Seeding Orchestration...\n");
  18 | 
  19 | 	await runSeed(db);
  20 | 	console.log("✅ Base Data (Clinic / Faker) Seeded");
  21 | 	console.log("--------------------------------------------------");
  22 | 
  23 | 	await drugSeed(db);
  24 | 	console.log("✅ NICU Drug Database Seeded");
  25 | 	console.log("--------------------------------------------------");
  26 | 
  27 | 	await wfaSeed(db);
  28 | 	console.log("✅ WHO WFA (JSON) Seeded");
  29 | 	console.log("--------------------------------------------------");
  30 | 
  31 | 	console.log("🎉 All seeds completed successfully!");
  32 | }
  33 | 
  34 | /**
  35 |  * Top-level execution
  36 |  */
  37 | (async () => {
  38 | 	try {
  39 | 		const { db, checkIsDbReady } = await import("./");
  40 | 		await checkIsDbReady();
  41 | 		await runAllSeeds(db);
  42 | 	} catch (error) {
  43 | 		console.error("❌ Master Seeding failed:", error);
  44 | 		process.exitCode = 1;
  45 | 	} finally {
  46 | 		// The postgres-js connection will close automatically on process exit
  47 | 		process.exit();
  48 | 	}
  49 | })();
```

`seed/seed-drugs.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { randomUUID } from "node:crypto";
   2 | import * as fs from "node:fs";
   3 | import * as path from "node:path";
   4 | 
   5 | import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
   6 | 
   7 | import type { DB as AppDb } from "../";
   8 | import { type DrugRoute, doseGuideline, drug as drugs } from "../schema";
   9 | 
  10 | /* =======================
  11 |    Types (unchanged)
  12 | ======================= */
  13 | 
  14 | type DoseGuidelineData = {
  15 | 	ROUTE: string;
  16 | 	CLINICAL_INDICATION: string;
  17 | 	MIN_DOSE_PER_KG: number | string;
  18 | 	MAX_DOSE_PER_KG: number | string;
  19 | 	DOSE_UNIT: string;
  20 | 	FREQUENCY_DAYS: string;
  21 | 	GESTATIONAL_AGE_WEEKS_MIN: number | string;
  22 | 	GESTATIONAL_AGE_WEEKS_MAX: number | string;
  23 | 	POST_NATAL_AGE_DAYS_MIN: number | string;
  24 | 	POST_NATAL_AGE_DAYS_MAX: number | string;
  25 | 	MAX_DOSE_PER_24H: number | string;
  26 | 	STOCK_CONCENTRATION_MG_ML: number | string;
  27 | 	FINAL_CONCENTRATION_MG_ML: number | string;
  28 | 	MIN_INFUSION_TIME_MIN: number | string;
  29 | 	COMPATIBILITY_DILUENT: string;
  30 | };
  31 | 
  32 | type DrugDatabase = {
  33 | 	[drugName: string]: DoseGuidelineData[];
  34 | };
  35 | 
  36 | /* =======================
  37 |    Helpers (unchanged)
  38 | ======================= */
  39 | 
  40 | function parseNumericValue(value: string | number): number | null {
  41 | 	if (value === "N/A" || value === "" || value == null) return null;
  42 | 	if (typeof value === "number") return value;
  43 | 	const parsed = Number.parseFloat(value.trim());
  44 | 	return Number.isNaN(parsed) ? null : parsed;
  45 | }
  46 | 
  47 | function parseIntegerValue(value: string | number): number | null {
  48 | 	if (value === "N/A" || value === "" || value == null) return null;
  49 | 	if (typeof value === "number") return Math.floor(value);
  50 | 	const parsed = Number.parseInt(value.trim(), 10);
  51 | 	return Number.isNaN(parsed) ? null : parsed;
  52 | }
  53 | 
  54 | const ROUTE_MAP: Record<string, DrugRoute> = {
  55 | 	PO: "ORAL",
  56 | 	ORAL: "ORAL",
  57 | 	IV: "INTRAVENOUS",
  58 | 	INTRAVENOUS: "INTRAVENOUS",
  59 | 	IM: "INTRAMUSCULAR",
  60 | 	INTRAMUSCULAR: "INTRAMUSCULAR",
  61 | 	SC: "SUBCUTANEOUS",
  62 | 	SUBCUTANEOUS: "SUBCUTANEOUS",
  63 | 	TOPICAL: "TOPICAL",
  64 | 	INHALATION: "INHALATION",
  65 | 	RECTAL: "RECTAL"
  66 | };
  67 | 
  68 | function normalizeDrugRoute(route: string): DrugRoute {
  69 | 	const normalized = ROUTE_MAP[route.trim().toUpperCase()];
  70 | 	if (!normalized) {
  71 | 		throw new Error(`Unsupported drug route in seed data: ${route}`);
  72 | 	}
  73 | 	return normalized;
  74 | }
  75 | 
  76 | /* =======================
  77 |    Drizzle Seed
  78 | ======================= */
  79 | 
  80 | export default async function drugSeed(db: AppDb) {
  81 | 	console.log("🌱 Starting NICU Drug Database seeding...");
  82 | 
  83 | 	const filePath = path.join(import.meta.dirname, "../../../data/nicu_data.json");
  84 | 	console.log(`📖 Reading data from: ${filePath}`);
  85 | 
  86 | 	const drugData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8")) as DrugDatabase;
  87 | 
  88 | 	const drugNames = Object.keys(drugData);
  89 | 	console.log(`📊 Found ${drugNames.length} drugs`);
  90 | 
  91 | 	const guidelinesBuffer: (typeof doseGuideline.$inferInsert)[] = [];
  92 | 	let totalGuidelines = 0;
  93 | 
  94 | 	for (const [drugName, guidelines] of Object.entries(drugData)) {
  95 | 		/* ---------- upsert drug ---------- */
  96 | 		const existingDrugs = await db.select().from(drugs).where(eq(drugs.name, drugName)).limit(1);
  97 | 		let drug = existingDrugs[0];
  98 | 
  99 | 		if (!drug) {
 100 | 			const id = randomUUID();
 101 | 			await db.insert(drugs).values({ id, name: drugName });
 102 | 			drug = {
 103 | 				id,
 104 | 				clinicId: null,
 105 | 				name: drugName,
 106 | 				genericName: null,
 107 | 				brandName: null,
 108 | 				description: null,
 109 | 				sideEffects: null,
 110 | 				quantityInStock: 0,
 111 | 				interactions: null,
 112 | 				contraindications: null,
 113 | 				createdAt: new Date(),
 114 | 				updatedAt: new Date()
 115 | 			};
 116 | 		}
 117 | 
 118 | 		/* ---------- collect guidelines ---------- */
 119 | 		for (const g of guidelines) {
 120 | 			guidelinesBuffer.push({
 121 | 				id: randomUUID(),
 122 | 				drugId: drug.id,
 123 | 				route: normalizeDrugRoute(g.ROUTE),
 124 | 				clinicalIndication: g.CLINICAL_INDICATION,
 125 | 
 126 | 				minDosePerKg: parseNumericValue(g.MIN_DOSE_PER_KG),
 127 | 				maxDosePerKg: parseNumericValue(g.MAX_DOSE_PER_KG),
 128 | 				doseUnit: g.DOSE_UNIT === "N/A" ? null : g.DOSE_UNIT,
 129 | 				frequencyDays: g.FREQUENCY_DAYS === "N/A" ? null : g.FREQUENCY_DAYS,
 130 | 
 131 | 				gestationalAgeWeeksMin: parseNumericValue(g.GESTATIONAL_AGE_WEEKS_MIN),
 132 | 				gestationalAgeWeeksMax: parseNumericValue(g.GESTATIONAL_AGE_WEEKS_MAX),
 133 | 
 134 | 				postNatalAgeDaysMin: parseIntegerValue(g.POST_NATAL_AGE_DAYS_MIN),
 135 | 				postNatalAgeDaysMax: parseIntegerValue(g.POST_NATAL_AGE_DAYS_MAX),
 136 | 
 137 | 				maxDosePer24h: parseNumericValue(g.MAX_DOSE_PER_24H),
 138 | 				stockConcentrationMgMl: parseNumericValue(g.STOCK_CONCENTRATION_MG_ML),
 139 | 				finalConcentrationMgMl: parseNumericValue(g.FINAL_CONCENTRATION_MG_ML),
 140 | 				minInfusionTimeMin: parseIntegerValue(g.MIN_INFUSION_TIME_MIN),
 141 | 
 142 | 				compatibilityDiluent: g.COMPATIBILITY_DILUENT === "N/A" ? null : g.COMPATIBILITY_DILUENT
 143 | 			});
 144 | 		}
 145 | 
 146 | 		totalGuidelines += guidelines.length;
 147 | 		console.log(`✅ ${drugName}: ${guidelines.length} guidelines`);
 148 | 	}
 149 | 
 150 | 	/* ---------- batch insert ---------- */
 151 | 	const BATCH_SIZE = 1000;
 152 | 	console.log(`⏳ Inserting ${guidelinesBuffer.length} guidelines...`);
 153 | 
 154 | 	for (let i = 0; i < guidelinesBuffer.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
 155 | 		await db.insert(doseGuideline).values(guidelinesBuffer.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE));
 156 | 	}
 157 | 
 158 | 	console.log("🎉 NICU Drug Database seeded successfully!");
 159 | 	console.log(`📈 Summary — Drugs: ${drugNames.length}, Guidelines: ${totalGuidelines}`);
 160 | }
```

`seed/seed-wfa.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { randomUUID } from "node:crypto";
   2 | import * as fs from "node:fs";
   3 | import * as path from "node:path";
   4 | 
   5 | import type { DB as AppDb } from "../";
   6 | import { whoGrowthStandard } from "../schema";
   7 | import { Gender } from "../seed/seed";
   8 | 
   9 | const ZSCORE_DATA_PATH = path.join(import.meta.dirname, "../../../data/zscore-wfa.json");
  10 | 
  11 | // const ZSCORE_DATA_PATH = path.join(__dirname,  "..","data", "zscore-wfa.json");
  12 | 
  13 | type ZScoreDataPoint = {
  14 | 	Day: string;
  15 | 	L: string;
  16 | 	M: string;
  17 | 	S: string;
  18 | 	SD4neg: string;
  19 | 	SD3neg: string;
  20 | 	SD2neg: string;
  21 | 	SD1neg: string;
  22 | 	SD0: string;
  23 | 	SD1: string;
  24 | 	SD2: string;
  25 | 	SD3: string;
  26 | 	SD4: string;
  27 | };
  28 | 
  29 | type GenderData = {
  30 | 	boys: ZScoreDataPoint[];
  31 | 	girls: ZScoreDataPoint[];
  32 | };
  33 | 
  34 | type ZScoreData = {
  35 | 	wfa: GenderData;
  36 | };
  37 | 
  38 | type ValidatedGrowthRecord = {
  39 | 	id: string;
  40 | 	ageInMonths: number;
  41 | 	ageDays: number;
  42 | 	gender: "MALE" | "FEMALE" | "OTHER";
  43 | 	measurementType: "WEIGHT" | "HEIGHT" | "BMI" | "HEAD_CIRCUMFERENCE";
  44 | 	lValue: number;
  45 | 	mValue: number;
  46 | 	sValue: number;
  47 | 	sd0: number;
  48 | 	sd1neg: number;
  49 | 	sd1pos: number;
  50 | 	sd2neg: number;
  51 | 	sd2pos: number;
  52 | 	sd3neg: number;
  53 | 	sd3pos: number;
  54 | 	sd4neg: number | null;
  55 | 	sd4pos: number | null;
  56 | 	createdAt: Date;
  57 | 	updatedAt: Date;
  58 | };
  59 | 
  60 | function parseNumericValue(value: string | undefined): number | null {
  61 | 	if (value === undefined || value.trim() === "") {
  62 | 		return null;
  63 | 	}
  64 | 	const parsed = Number.parseFloat(value);
  65 | 	return Number.isNaN(parsed) ? null : parsed;
  66 | }
  67 | 
  68 | function calculateAgeInMonths(ageDays: number): number {
  69 | 	// Calculate age in months with better precision
  70 | 	return Number.parseFloat((ageDays / 30.4375).toFixed(2)); // Keep 2 decimal places for accuracy
  71 | }
  72 | 
  73 | function mapDataPoint(dataPoint: ZScoreDataPoint, gender: Gender): ValidatedGrowthRecord {
  74 | 	const ageDaysRaw = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.Day);
  75 | 	if (ageDaysRaw === null) {
  76 | 		throw new Error(`Invalid 'Day' value: ${dataPoint.Day}`);
  77 | 	}
  78 | 	const ageDays = Math.round(ageDaysRaw);
  79 | 	const ageInMonths = calculateAgeInMonths(ageDays);
  80 | 
  81 | 	const lValue = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.L);
  82 | 	const mValue = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.M);
  83 | 	const sValue = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.S);
  84 | 	const sd0 = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD0);
  85 | 	const sd1neg = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD1neg);
  86 | 	const sd1pos = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD1);
  87 | 	const sd2neg = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD2neg);
  88 | 	const sd2pos = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD2);
  89 | 	const sd3neg = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD3neg);
  90 | 	const sd3pos = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD3);
  91 | 	const sd4neg = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD4neg);
  92 | 	const sd4pos = parseNumericValue(dataPoint.SD4);
  93 | 
  94 | 	const requiredFields = {
  95 | 		lValue,
  96 | 		mValue,
  97 | 		sValue,
  98 | 		sd0,
  99 | 		sd1neg,
 100 | 		sd1pos,
 101 | 		sd2neg,
 102 | 		sd2pos,
 103 | 		sd3neg,
 104 | 		sd3pos
 105 | 	};
 106 | 
 107 | 	for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(requiredFields)) {
 108 | 		if (value === null) {
 109 | 			throw new Error(`Missing or invalid required numeric field: ${key}`);
 110 | 		}
 111 | 	}
 112 | 
 113 | 	const validatedFields = requiredFields as Record<keyof typeof requiredFields, number>;
 114 | 
 115 | 	return {
 116 | 		id: randomUUID(),
 117 | 		ageInMonths,
 118 | 		ageDays,
 119 | 		gender: gender as "MALE" | "FEMALE" | "OTHER",
 120 | 		measurementType: "WEIGHT", // WFA maps to WEIGHT in the schema enum
 121 | 		lValue: validatedFields.lValue,
 122 | 		mValue: validatedFields.mValue,
 123 | 		sValue: validatedFields.sValue,
 124 | 		sd0: validatedFields.sd0,
 125 | 		sd1neg: validatedFields.sd1neg,
 126 | 		sd1pos: validatedFields.sd1pos,
 127 | 		sd2neg: validatedFields.sd2neg,
 128 | 		sd2pos: validatedFields.sd2pos,
 129 | 		sd3neg: validatedFields.sd3neg,
 130 | 		sd3pos: validatedFields.sd3pos,
 131 | 		sd4neg,
 132 | 		sd4pos,
 133 | 		createdAt: new Date(),
 134 | 		updatedAt: new Date()
 135 | 	};
 136 | }
 137 | 
 138 | export default async function wfaSeed(db: AppDb) {
 139 | 	console.log("--- Starting WHO Growth Standards Seeding ---");
 140 | 
 141 | 	let whoJson: ZScoreData;
 142 | 	try {
 143 | 		whoJson = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(ZSCORE_DATA_PATH, "utf-8")) as ZScoreData;
 144 | 		if (!whoJson?.wfa) {
 145 | 			throw new Error("JSON file is missing required 'wfa' data.");
 146 | 		}
 147 | 	} catch (error) {
 148 | 		console.error(error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error");
 149 | 		return;
 150 | 	}
 151 | 
 152 | 	const allRecords: ValidatedGrowthRecord[] = [];
 153 | 	let recordsSkipped = 0;
 154 | 
 155 | 	console.log("Processing wfa data...");
 156 | 
 157 | 	// Process boys data
 158 | 	if (whoJson.wfa.boys && Array.isArray(whoJson.wfa.boys)) {
 159 | 		console.log(`  Processing ${whoJson.wfa.boys.length} boys records...`);
 160 | 		let boysProcessed = 0;
 161 | 		let boysSkipped = 0;
 162 | 		// FIX 1: Replace forEach with for...of
 163 | 		for (const dataPoint of whoJson.wfa.boys) {
 164 | 			try {
 165 | 				const mappedRecord = mapDataPoint(dataPoint, Gender.MALE);
 166 | 				allRecords.push(mappedRecord);
 167 | 				boysProcessed += 1; // FIX 2: Replace ++
 168 | 			} catch (error) {
 169 | 				boysSkipped += 1; // FIX 3: Replace ++
 170 | 				recordsSkipped += 1; // FIX 4: Replace ++
 171 | 				console.warn(`Skipping boys record Day ${dataPoint.Day}: ${error}`);
 172 | 			}
 173 | 		}
 174 | 		console.log(`    ✅ Processed: ${boysProcessed}, ❌ Skipped: ${boysSkipped}`);
 175 | 	}
 176 | 
 177 | 	// Process girls data
 178 | 	if (whoJson.wfa.girls && Array.isArray(whoJson.wfa.girls)) {
 179 | 		console.log(`  Processing ${whoJson.wfa.girls.length} girls records...`);
 180 | 		let girlsProcessed = 0;
 181 | 		let girlsSkipped = 0;
 182 | 
 183 | 		// FIX 5: Replace forEach with for...of
 184 | 		for (const dataPoint of whoJson.wfa.girls) {
 185 | 			try {
 186 | 				const mappedRecord = mapDataPoint(dataPoint, Gender.FEMALE);
 187 | 				allRecords.push(mappedRecord);
 188 | 				girlsProcessed += 1; // FIX 6: Replace ++
 189 | 			} catch (error) {
 190 | 				girlsSkipped += 1; // FIX 7: Replace ++
 191 | 				recordsSkipped += 1; // FIX 8: Replace ++
 192 | 				console.warn(`Skipping girls record Day ${dataPoint.Day}: ${error}`);
 193 | 			}
 194 | 		}
 195 | 		console.log(`    ✅ Processed: ${girlsProcessed}, ❌ Skipped: ${girlsSkipped}`);
 196 | 	}
 197 | 
 198 | 	console.log(`\nTotal records successfully mapped: ${allRecords.length}`);
 199 | 
 200 | 	if (recordsSkipped > 0) {
 201 | 		console.log(`Records skipped due to errors: ${recordsSkipped}`);
 202 | 	}
 203 | 
 204 | 	// Check for duplicates using ageDays + gender + measurementType
 205 | 	const uniqueRecordsMap = new Map<string, ValidatedGrowthRecord>();
 206 | 	const duplicates: string[] = [];
 207 | 
 208 | 	for (const record of allRecords) {
 209 | 		// Use ageDays as the unique identifier along with gender and measurementType
 210 | 		const key = `${record.gender}:${record.measurementType}:${record.ageDays}`;
 211 | 
 212 | 		if (uniqueRecordsMap.has(key)) {
 213 | 			duplicates.push(key);
 214 | 			console.warn(`⚠️ Duplicate found: ${key} (Age: ${record.ageInMonths} months)`);
 215 | 		} else {
 216 | 			uniqueRecordsMap.set(key, record);
 217 | 		}
 218 | 	}
 219 | 
 220 | 	const dataToInsert = Array.from(uniqueRecordsMap.values());
 221 | 
 222 | 	console.log(`\nUnique records ready for insertion: ${dataToInsert.length}`);
 223 | 	if (duplicates.length > 0) {
 224 | 		console.log(`Actual duplicates found and removed: ${duplicates.length}`);
 225 | 	}
 226 | 
 227 | 	// Show sample age calculations
 228 | 	console.log("\n📏 Sample Age Calculations:");
 229 | 	const sampleAges = [0, 30, 365, 1000, 1856]; // Sample days
 230 | 
 231 | 	// FIX 9: Replace forEach with for...of
 232 | 	for (const days of sampleAges) {
 233 | 		const months = calculateAgeInMonths(days);
 234 | 		console.log(`  ${days} days = ${months.toFixed(2)} months`);
 235 | 	}
 236 | 
 237 | 	// Clear existing data
 238 | 
 239 | 	console.log("\nClearing existing WHO growth standard data...");
 240 | 
 241 | 	try {
 242 | 		await db.delete(whoGrowthStandard).execute();
 243 | 		console.log("✅ Existing data cleared.");
 244 | 	} catch (error) {
 245 | 		console.error("❌ Could not clear existing data:", error);
 246 | 		return;
 247 | 	}
 248 | 	// Perform Bulk Insertion
 249 | 	if (dataToInsert.length > 0) {
 250 | 		try {
 251 | 			const batchSize = 1000;
 252 | 			let totalInserted = 0;
 253 | 
 254 | 			for (let i = 0; i < dataToInsert.length; i += batchSize) {
 255 | 				const batch = dataToInsert.slice(i, i + batchSize);
 256 | 				const batchNumber = Math.floor(i / batchSize) + 1;
 257 | 
 258 | 				console.log(`\nInserting batch ${batchNumber} (${batch.length} records)...`);
 259 | 
 260 | 				await db.insert(whoGrowthStandard).values(batch).execute();
 261 | 
 262 | 				totalInserted += batch.length;
 263 | 
 264 | 				console.log(`  ✅ Inserted ${batch.length} records in batch ${batchNumber}.`);
 265 | 			}
 266 | 
 267 | 			console.log(`\n🎉 SUCCESS! Inserted ${totalInserted} total WHO Growth Standard records.`);
 268 | 
 269 | 			const summary = {
 270 | 				"Boys records": whoJson.wfa.boys?.length || 0,
 271 | 				"Girls records": whoJson.wfa.girls?.length || 0,
 272 | 				"Total expected": (whoJson.wfa.boys?.length || 0) + (whoJson.wfa.girls?.length || 0),
 273 | 				"Successfully processed": allRecords.length,
 274 | 				"Skipped due to errors": recordsSkipped,
 275 | 				"Actual duplicates removed": duplicates.length,
 276 | 				"Final inserted": totalInserted
 277 | 			};
 278 | 
 279 | 			console.log("\n📊 Seeding Summary:");
 280 | 			for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(summary)) {
 281 | 				console.log(`  ${key}: ${value}`);
 282 | 			}
 283 | 		} catch (error) {
 284 | 			console.error("❌ Failed to insert WHO Growth Standard records:", error);
 285 | 		}
 286 | 	} else {
 287 | 		console.log("⚠️ No valid WHO Growth Standard data was mapped for insertion.");
 288 | 	}
 289 | }

```
`seed/seed.ts`:

```ts
   1 | /** biome-ignore-all lint/complexity/noExcessiveCognitiveComplexity: <seed> */
   2 | /** biome-ignore-all lint/suspicious/noExplicitAny: <seed> */
   3 | 
   4 | import { faker } from "@faker-js/faker";
   5 | 
   6 | import type { DB } from "../";
   7 | import {
   8 | 	account,
   9 | 	appointment,
  10 | 	clinic,
  11 | 	clinicMember,
  12 | 	clinicSetting,
  13 | 	configStore,
  14 | 	type DbAppointment,
  15 | 	type DbDiagnosis,
  16 | 	type DbMedicalRecord,
  17 | 	type DbPatient,

 215 | // Helper functions
 216 | const getRandomEnumValue = <T>(enumObj: Record<string, T>): T => {
 217 | 	const enumValues = Object.values(enumObj) as T[];
 218 | 	if (enumValues.length === 0) {
 219 | 		throw new Error("Enum object has no values");
 220 | 	}
 221 | 	const index = Math.floor(Math.random() * enumValues.length);
 222 | 	const value = enumValues[index];
 223 | 	if (value === undefined) {
 224 | 		throw new Error("Failed to pick a random enum value");
 225 | 	}
 226 | 	return value;
 227 | };
 228 | 
 229 | const getRandomSubset = <T>(array: T[], count: number): T[] => {
 230 | 	const shuffled = [...array].sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
 231 | 	return shuffled.slice(0, Math.min(count, shuffled.length));
 232 | };
 233 | 
 234 | const weightedRandom = <T>(items: Array<{ item: T; weight: number }>): T => {
 235 | 	const total = items.reduce((sum, { weight }) => sum + weight, 0);
 236 | 	let random = Math.random() * total;
 237 | 
 238 | 	if (items.length === 0) {
 239 | 		throw new Error("weightedRandom called with empty items");
 240 | 	}
 241 | 
 242 | 	for (const { item, weight } of items) {
 243 | 		if (random < weight) return item;
 244 | 		random -= weight;
 245 | 	}
 246 | 
 247 | 	const fallbackItem = items[0];
 248 | 	if (fallbackItem === undefined) {
 249 | 		throw new Error("weightedRandom: items[0] is undefined");
 250 | 	}
 251 | 	return fallbackItem.item;
 252 | };
 253 | 
 254 | // Time helper functions
 255 | const randomTime = (): string => {
 256 | 	const hours = faker.number.int({ min: 8, max: 17 }).toString().padStart(2, "0");
 257 | 	const minutes = faker.helpers.arrayElement(["00", "15", "30", "45"]);
 258 | 	return `${hours}:${minutes}`;
 259 | };
 260 | 
 261 | // Generate realistic date of birth based on patient type
 262 | const generateDateOfBirth = (patientType: "adult" | "child" | "infant"): Date => {
 263 | 	switch (patientType) {
 264 | 		case "infant":
 265 | 			return faker.date.birthdate({ min: 0, max: 2, mode: "age" });
 266 | 		case "child":
 267 | 			return faker.date.birthdate({ min: 2, max: 18, mode: "age" });
 268 | 		default: // adult
 269 | 			return faker.date.birthdate({ min: 18, max: 90, mode: "age" });
 270 | 	}
 271 | };
 272 | 
 273 | // Helper function to safely delete data
 274 | const safeDeleteMany = async (db: DB, table: Parameters<DB["delete"]>[0]): Promise<void> => {
 275 | 	try {
 276 | 		await db.delete(table);
 277 | 	} catch (err: unknown) {
 278 | 		const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
 279 | 		if (errMsg.includes("no such table") || errMsg.includes("does not exist")) {
 280 | 			return;
 281 | 		}
 282 | 		throw err;
 283 | 	}
 284 | };

 286 | // Function to clear all data in proper order (respecting foreign key constraints)
 287 | const clearAllData = async (db: DB) => {
 288 | 	console.log("🗑️ Clearing existing data in proper order...");
 289 | 
 290 | 	// Clear data in reverse order of dependencies
 291 | 	const clearOperations = [
 292 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, prescribedItem),
 293 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, prescription),
 294 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, doseGuideline),
 295 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, drug),
 296 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, vitalSign),
 297 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, diagnosis),
 298 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, labTest),
 299 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, patientBill),
 300 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, payment),
 301 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, reminder),
 302 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, feedingLog),
 303 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, immunization),
 304 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, developmentalMilestones),
 305 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, developmentalCheck),
 306 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, rating),
 307 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, medicalRecord),
 308 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, appointment),
 309 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, workingDay),
 310 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, service),
 311 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, guardian),
 312 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, growthRecord),
 313 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, whoGrowthStandard),
 314 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, vaccineSchedule),
 315 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, staff),
 316 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, doctor),
 317 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, patient),
 318 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, clinicMember),
 319 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, clinicSetting),
 320 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, clinic),
 321 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, verification),
 322 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, account),
 323 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, session),
 324 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, userQuota),
 325 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, invite),
 326 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, twoFactor),
 327 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, folder),
 328 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, file),
 329 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, configStore),
 330 | 		() => safeDeleteMany(db, user)
 331 | 	];
 332 | 
 333 | 	for (const operation of clearOperations) {
 334 | 		await operation();
 335 | 	}
 336 | };

 338 | // Create realistic clinics
 339 | async function createClinics(db: DB) {
 340 | 	console.log("🏥 Creating clinics...");
 341 | 	const clinicsData: (typeof clinic.$inferSelect)[] = [];
 342 | 	const clinicNames = [
 343 | 		"City Medical Center",
 344 | 		"Community Health Clinic",
 345 | 		"Family Care Hospital",
 346 | 		"Pediatric Specialists",
 347 | 		"General Healthcare Clinic",
 348 | 		"Metropolitan Hospital",
 349 | 		"Sunrise Medical Center",
 350 | 		"Children's Health Center"
 351 | 	];
 352 | 
 353 | 	for (const name of clinicNames) {
 354 | 		const clinicData = {
 355 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
 356 | 			name,
 357 | 			email: faker.internet.email({
 358 | 				firstName: (name.split(" ")[0] ?? "clinic").toLowerCase()
 359 | 			}),
 360 | 			timezone: faker.helpers.arrayElement(["UTC", "America/New_York", "Europe/London", "Asia/Tokyo"]),
 361 | 			address: faker.location.streetAddress(),
 362 | 			phone: faker.phone.number(),
 363 | 			isDefault: false,
 364 | 			deletedAt: null,
 365 | 			isDeleted: false,
 366 | 			createdAt: faker.date.past({ years: 2 }),
 367 | 			updatedAt: faker.date.past({ years: 2 })
 368 | 		};
 369 | 
 370 | 		await db.insert(clinic).values(clinicData);
 371 | 		clinicsData.push(clinicData);
 372 | 
 373 | 		// Create clinic settings
 374 | 		await db.insert(clinicSetting).values({
 375 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
 376 | 			clinicId: clinicData.id,
 377 | 			openingTime: "08:00",
 378 | 			closingTime: "17:00",
 379 | 			workingDays: "MON,TUE,WED,THU,FRI,SAT",
 380 | 			defaultAppointmentDuration: faker.helpers.arrayElement([15, 30, 45, 60]),
 381 | 			requireEmergencyContact: faker.datatype.boolean(),
 382 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
 383 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
 384 | 		});
 385 | 	}
 386 | 
 387 | 	return clinicsData;
 388 | }

 454 | 		};

 513 | // Associate users with clinics
 514 | async function associateUsersWithClinics(
 515 | 	db: DB,
 516 | 	users: (typeof user.$inferSelect)[],
 517 | 	clinicsData: (typeof clinic.$inferSelect)[]
 518 | ) {
 519 | 	console.log("🔗 Associating users with clinics...");
 520 | 
 521 | 	for (const user of users) {
 522 | 		const userClinics = getRandomSubset(clinicsData, 1);
 523 | 		for (const clinic of userClinics) {
 524 | 			await db.insert(clinicMember).values({
 525 | 				userId: user.id,
 526 | 				clinicId: clinic.id,
 527 | 				role: (user.role ?? "patient") as "admin" | "doctor" | "staff" | "patient",
 528 | 				createdAt: faker.date.past({ years: 1 }),
 529 | 				updatedAt: faker.date.past({ years: 1 })
 530 | 			});
 531 | 		}
 532 | 	}
 533 | }

 535 | // Create doctors with realistic data
 536 | async function createDoctors(db: DB, users: (typeof user.$inferSelect)[], clinicsData: (typeof clinic.$inferSelect)[]) {
 537 | 	console.log("👨‍⚕️ Creating doctors...");
 538 | 	const doctors: (typeof doctor.$inferSelect)[] = [];
 539 | 	const doctorUsers = users.filter(user => user.role === "doctor");
 540 | 
 541 | 	const specialties = [
 542 | 		"Pediatrics",
 543 | 		"Cardiology",
 544 | 		"Dermatology",
 545 | 		"Neurology",
 546 | 		"Orthopedics",
 547 | 		"Gynecology",
 548 | 		"Psychiatry",
 549 | 		"General Medicine",
 550 | 		"Surgery",
 551 | 		"Oncology",
 552 | 		"Endocrinology",
 553 | 		"Gastroenterology",
 554 | 		"Pulmonology",
 555 | 		"Rheumatology",
 556 | 		"Urology"
 557 | 	];
 558 | 
 559 | 	for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(CONFIG.totalDoctors, doctorUsers.length); i++) {
 560 | 		const user = doctorUsers[i];
 561 | 		if (!user) continue;
 562 | 
 563 | 		const clinic = faker.helpers.arrayElement(clinicsData);
 564 | 		const specialty = faker.helpers.arrayElement(specialties);
 565 | 
 566 | 		const doctorData = {
 567 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
 568 | 			email: user.email ?? "",
 569 | 			name: user.name,
 570 | 			userId: user.id,
 571 | 			clinicId: clinic.id,
 572 | 			specialty,
 573 | 			licenseNumber: faker.string.alphanumeric(10).toUpperCase(),
 574 | 			phone: faker.phone.number(),
 575 | 			address: faker.location.streetAddress(),
 576 | 			department: faker.helpers.arrayElement(["Emergency", "Outpatient", "Surgery", "ICU", "Pediatrics"]),
 577 | 			img: faker.image.avatar(),
 578 | 			colorCode: faker.color.rgb(),
 579 | 			availabilityStatus: weightedRandom([
 580 | 				{ item: AvailabilityStatus.AVAILABLE, weight: 0.6 },
 581 | 				{ item: AvailabilityStatus.UNAVAILABLE, weight: 0.2 },
 582 | 				{ item: AvailabilityStatus.ON_LEAVE, weight: 0.2 }
 583 | 			]),
 584 | 			availableFromWeekDay: faker.helpers.arrayElement(WEEKDAYS),
 585 | 			availableToWeekDay: faker.helpers.arrayElement(WEEKDAYS),
 586 | 			availableFromTime: "08:00",
 587 | 			availableToTime: "18:00",
 588 | 			type: getRandomEnumValue(DoctorType),
 589 | 			appointmentPrice: faker.number.int({ min: 80, max: 300 }),
 590 | 			status: weightedRandom([
 591 | 				{ item: Status.ACTIVE, weight: 0.85 },
 592 | 				{ item: Status.INACTIVE, weight: 0.1 },
 593 | 				{ item: Status.ON_HOLD, weight: 0.05 }
 594 | 			]),
 595 | 			isActive: faker.datatype.boolean(0.9),
 596 | 			role: "doctor" as const,
 597 | 			rating: faker.number.int({ min: 1, max: 5 }),
 598 | 			isDeleted: false,
 599 | 			deletedAt: null,
 600 | 			createdAt: faker.date.past({ years: 2 }),
 601 | 			updatedAt: faker.date.past({ years: 2 })
 602 | 		};
 603 | 
 604 | 		await db.insert(doctor).values(doctorData);
 605 | 		doctors.push(doctorData);
 606 | 
 607 | 		// Create working days
 608 | 		const workingDayList = getRandomSubset([...WEEKDAYS], faker.number.int({ min: 4, max: 6 }));
 609 | 
 610 | 		for (const day of workingDayList) {
 611 | 			await db.insert(workingDay).values({
 612 | 				id: faker.string.uuid(),
 613 | 				doctorId: doctorData.id,
 614 | 				day,

 878 | // Create appointments
 879 | async function createAppointments(
 880 | 	db: DB,
 881 | 	patients: (typeof patient.$inferSelect)[],
 882 | 	doctors: (typeof doctor.$inferSelect)[],
 883 | 	services: (typeof service.$inferSelect)[]
 884 | ) {
 885 | 	console.log("📅 Creating appointments...");
 886 | 	const appointments: (typeof appointment.$inferSelect)[] = [];
 887 | 
 888 | 	for (let i = 0; i < CONFIG.totalAppointments; i++) {
 889 | 		const patient = faker.helpers.arrayElement(patients);
 890 | 		const doctor = faker.helpers.arrayElement(doctors);
 891 | 		const service = faker.helpers.arrayElement(services);
 892 | 		const clinicId = doctor.clinicId
 893 | 			? doctor.clinicId
 894 | 			: (faker.helpers.arrayElement([...new Set(patients.map(p => p.clinicId))]) ?? "");
 895 | 
 896 | 		const status = weightedRandom([
 897 | 			{ item: AppointmentStatus.CONFIRMED, weight: 0.4 },
 898 | 			{ item: AppointmentStatus.COMPLETED, weight: 0.4 },
 899 | 			{ item: AppointmentStatus.CANCELLED, weight: 0.15 },
 900 | 			{ item: AppointmentStatus.PENDING, weight: 0.05 }
 901 | 		]);
 902 | 
 903 | 		let appointmentDate: Date;
 904 | 		if (status === AppointmentStatus.COMPLETED) {
 905 | 			appointmentDate = faker.date.past({ years: 1 });
 906 | 		} else if (status === AppointmentStatus.CONFIRMED) {
 907 | 			appointmentDate = faker.date.future({ years: 0.5 });
 908 | 		} else {
 909 | 			const fromDate = faker.date.past({ years: 1 });
 910 | 			const toDate = faker.date.future({ years: 0.5 });
 911 | 			appointmentDate = faker.date.between({ from: fromDate, to: toDate });
 912 | 		}
 913 | 
 914 | 		const appointmentData = {
 915 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
 916 | 			patientId: patient.id,
 917 | 			doctorId: doctor.id,
 918 | 			serviceId: service.id,
 919 | 			doctorSpecialty: doctor.specialty,
 920 | 			appointmentDate,
 921 | 			appointmentPrice: doctor.appointmentPrice,
 922 | 			clinicId,
 923 | 			durationMinutes: faker.number.int({ min: 30, max: 120 }),
 924 | 			time: randomTime(),
 925 | 			status: status as AppointmentStatus,
 926 | 			type: weightedRandom([
 927 | 				{ item: "Checkup", weight: 0.5 },
 928 | 				{ item: "Follow-up", weight: 0.3 },
 929 | 				{ item: "Emergency", weight: 0.1 },
 930 | 				{ item: "Consultation", weight: 0.1 }
 931 | 			]),
 932 | 			note: faker.datatype.boolean(0.7) ? faker.lorem.sentence() : null,
 933 | 			reason: faker.datatype.boolean(0.8) ? faker.lorem.sentence() : null,
 934 | 			isDeleted: false,
 935 | 			deletedAt: null,
 936 | 			createdAt: faker.date.past({ years: 1 }),
 937 | 			updatedAt: faker.date.past({ years: 1 })
 938 | 		};
 939 | 
 940 | 		await db.insert(appointment).values(appointmentData);
 941 | 		appointments.push(appointmentData);
 942 | 
 943 | 		// Create reminders for upcoming appointments
 944 | 		if (status === AppointmentStatus.CONFIRMED && appointmentDate > new Date()) {
 945 | 			await createReminder(db, appointmentData);
 946 | 		}
 947 | 	}
 948 | 
 949 | 	return appointments;
 950 | }
 951 | 
 952 | // Create reminder for appointment
 953 | const createReminder = async (db: DB, appointment: DbAppointment) => {
 954 | 	if (faker.datatype.boolean(0.6)) {
 955 | 		await db.insert(reminder).values({
 956 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
 957 | 			appointmentId: appointment.id,
 958 | 			method: getRandomEnumValue(ReminderMethod),
 959 | 			sentAt: faker.date.recent(),
 960 | 			status: weightedRandom([
 961 | 				{ item: ReminderStatus.SENT, weight: 0.8 },
 962 | 				{ item: ReminderStatus.FAILED, weight: 0.1 },
 963 | 				{ item: ReminderStatus.PENDING, weight: 0.1 }
 964 | 			])
 965 | 		});
 966 | 	}
 967 | };

 969 | // Create medical records and related data
 970 | async function createMedicalRecords(
 971 | 	db: DB,
 972 | 	patients: (typeof patient.$inferSelect)[],
 973 | 	appointments: (typeof appointment.$inferSelect)[],
 974 | 	services: (typeof service.$inferSelect)[]
 975 | ) {
 976 | 	console.log("📋 Creating medical records & related data...");
 977 | 	const medicalRecords: (typeof medicalRecord.$inferSelect & {
 978 | 		encounterId?: string;
 979 | 	})[] = [];
 980 | 
 981 | 	// Use only completed appointments for medical records
 982 | 	const completedAppointments = appointments.filter(a => a.status === AppointmentStatus.COMPLETED);
 983 | 
 984 | 	for (const appointment of getRandomSubset(completedAppointments, CONFIG.totalMedicalRecords)) {
 985 | 		const patient = patients.find(p => p.id === appointment.patientId);
 986 | 		if (!patient) continue;
 987 | 
 988 | 		const medicalRecordData = {
 989 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
 990 | 			patientId: appointment.patientId ?? "",
 991 | 			appointmentId: appointment.id,
 992 | 			doctorId: appointment.doctorId,
 993 | 			treatmentPlan: faker.datatype.boolean(0.8) ? faker.lorem.paragraph() : null,
 994 | 			labRequest: faker.datatype.boolean(0.5) ? faker.lorem.sentence() : null,
 995 | 			clinicId: appointment.clinicId ?? "",
 996 | 			diagnosis: faker.datatype.boolean(0.7) ? faker.lorem.words(faker.number.int({ min: 1, max: 3 })) : null,
 997 | 			symptoms: faker.datatype.boolean(0.8) ? faker.lorem.words(faker.number.int({ min: 1, max: 5 })) : null,
 998 | 			notes: faker.datatype.boolean(0.6) ? faker.lorem.paragraph() : null,
 999 | 			attachments: faker.datatype.boolean(0.3) ? faker.system.filePath() : null,
1000 | 			followUpDate: faker.datatype.boolean(0.4) ? faker.date.future({ years: 0.5 }) : null,
1001 | 			isDeleted: false,
1002 | 			deletedAt: null,
1003 | 			status: (faker.datatype.boolean(0.8) ? "COMPLETED" : "PENDING") as Status,
1004 | 			diagnosisDate: faker.date.past({ years: 0.5 }),
1005 | 			medications: faker.datatype.boolean(0.5) ? faker.lorem.words(faker.number.int({ min: 1, max: 3 })) : null,
1006 | 			createdAt: appointment.appointmentDate,
1007 | 			updatedAt: appointment.appointmentDate
1008 | 		};
1009 | 
1010 | 		await db.insert(medicalRecord).values(medicalRecordData);
1011 | 
1012 | 		try {
1013 | 			// Create encounter (diagnosis)
1014 | 			const encounter = await createDiagnosis(db, medicalRecordData, appointment);
1015 | 			medicalRecords.push({ ...medicalRecordData, encounterId: encounter.id });
1016 | 			// Create vital signs
1017 | 			if (faker.datatype.boolean(0.8)) {
1018 | 				await createVitalSigns(db, patient, medicalRecordData, encounter);
1019 | 			}
1020 | 
1021 | 			if (faker.datatype.boolean(0.4)) {
1022 | 				await createLabTest(db, medicalRecordData, services);
1023 | 			}
1024 | 		} catch (error) {
1025 | 			console.error("Failed to create related data for medical record:", medicalRecordData.id, error);
1026 | 			throw error;
1027 | 		}
1028 | 	}
1029 | 
1030 | 	return medicalRecords;
1031 | }

1044 | 			{ item: "Follow-up", weight: 0.4 },
1045 | 			{ item: "Emergency", weight: 0.1 },
1046 | 			{ item: "Consultation", weight: 0.1 }
1047 | 		]),

1050 | 		notes: medicalRecord.notes,

1054 | 		status: "COMPLETED" as Status,
1055 | 		followUpPlan: faker.datatype.boolean(0.6) ? faker.lorem.sentence() : null,
1056 | 		isDeleted: false,

1066 | // Create vital signs
1067 | const createVitalSigns = async (db: DB, patient: DbPatient, medicalRecord: DbMedicalRecord, encounter: DbDiagnosis) => {
1068 | 	const ageDays = Math.floor((Date.now() - (patient.dateOfBirth as Date).getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
1069 | 	const ageMonths = Math.floor(ageDays / 30);
1070 | 
1071 | 	const vitalSignsData = {
1072 | 		id: faker.string.uuid(),
1073 | 		clinicId: medicalRecord.clinicId,
1074 | 		encounterId: encounter.id,
1075 | 		patientId: patient.id,
1076 | 		medicalId: medicalRecord.id,
1077 | 		growthRecordId: null,
1078 | 		recordedAt: encounter.date ?? medicalRecord.createdAt,
1079 | 		gender: patient.gender,
1080 | 		ageDays,
1081 | 		ageMonths,
1082 | 		notes: faker.datatype.boolean(0.3) ? faker.lorem.sentence() : null,
1083 | 		bodyTemperature: null as number | null,
1084 | 		systolic: null as number | null,
1085 | 		diastolic: null as number | null,
1086 | 		heartRate: null as number | null,
1087 | 		respiratoryRate: null as number | null,
1088 | 		oxygenSaturation: null as number | null,
1089 | 		createdAt: new Date(),
1090 | 		updatedAt: new Date()
1091 | 	};
1092 | 
1093 | 	const growthRecordData = {
1094 | 		id: faker.string.uuid(),
1095 | 		clinicId: medicalRecord.clinicId,
1096 | 		patientId: patient.id,
1097 | 		recordedAt: encounter.date ?? medicalRecord.createdAt,
1098 | 		height: null as number | null,
1099 | 		weight: null as number | null,
1100 | 		bmi: null as number | null,
1101 | 		date: encounter.date ?? medicalRecord.createdAt,
1102 | 		headCircumference: null as number | null,
1103 | 		notes: null as string | null,
1104 | 		gender: patient.gender,
1105 | 		ageDays,
1106 | 		ageMonths,
1107 | 		weightForAgeZ: null as number | null,
1108 | 		heightForAgeZ: null as number | null,
1109 | 		bmiForAgeZ: null as number | null,
1110 | 		hcForAgeZ: null as number | null,
1111 | 		createdAt: new Date(),
1112 | 		updatedAt: new Date()
1113 | 	};
1114 | 
1115 | 	// Add vitals based on patient age
1116 | 	if (ageMonths < 24) {
1117 | 		// Infant/child
1118 | 		vitalSignsData.bodyTemperature = faker.number.float({
1119 | 			min: 36.5,
1120 | 			max: 37.5
1121 | 		});
1122 | 		growthRecordData.height = faker.number.float({
1123 | 			min: 45,
1124 | 			max: 100
1125 | 		});
1126 | 		growthRecordData.weight = faker.number.float({
1127 | 			min: 2.5,
1128 | 			max: 20
1129 | 		});
1130 | 		growthRecordData.headCircumference = faker.number.float({
1131 | 			min: 30,
1132 | 			max: 50
1133 | 		});
1134 | 	} else {
1135 | 		// Adult
1136 | 		vitalSignsData.bodyTemperature = faker.number.float({
1137 | 			min: 36.0,
1138 | 			max: 37.5
1139 | 		});
1140 | 		growthRecordData.height = faker.number.float({
1141 | 			min: 150,
1142 | 			max: 200
1143 | 		});
1144 | 		growthRecordData.weight = faker.number.float({
1145 | 			min: 45,
1146 | 			max: 120
1147 | 		});
1148 | 		vitalSignsData.systolic = faker.number.int({ min: 100, max: 140 });
1149 | 		vitalSignsData.diastolic = faker.number.int({ min: 60, max: 90 });
1150 | 
1151 | 		vitalSignsData.heartRate = faker.number.int({ min: 60, max: 100 });
1152 | 		vitalSignsData.respiratoryRate = faker.number.int({ min: 12, max: 20 });
1153 | 		vitalSignsData.oxygenSaturation = faker.number.int({ min: 95, max: 100 });
1154 | 
1155 | 		// Calculate BMI
1156 | 		if (growthRecordData.height && growthRecordData.weight) {
1157 | 			const heightInM = growthRecordData.height / 100;
1158 | 			growthRecordData.bmi = growthRecordData.weight / (heightInM * heightInM);
1159 | 		}
1160 | 
1161 | 		// Calculate WHO percentiles for children if under 5 years
1162 | 		if (ageMonths < 60 && growthRecordData.height && growthRecordData.weight) {
1163 | 			growthRecordData.weightForAgeZ = faker.number.float({
1164 | 				min: -2,
1165 | 				max: 2
1166 | 			});
1167 | 			growthRecordData.heightForAgeZ = faker.number.float({
1168 | 				min: -2,
1169 | 				max: 2
1170 | 			});
1171 | 			growthRecordData.bmiForAgeZ = faker.number.float({
1172 | 				min: -2,
1173 | 				max: 2
1174 | 			});
1175 | 			growthRecordData.hcForAgeZ = growthRecordData.headCircumference
1176 | 				? faker.number.float({ min: -2, max: 2 })
1177 | 				: null;
1178 | 		}
1179 | 	}
1180 | 
1181 | 	await db.insert(vitalSign).values(vitalSignsData);
1182 | 	await db.insert(growthRecord).values(growthRecordData);
1183 | };

1328 | // Create payments
1329 | const createPayments = async (
1330 | 	db: DB,
1331 | 	appointments: (typeof appointment.$inferSelect)[],
1332 | 	patients: DbPatient[],
1333 | 	services: DbService[]
1334 | ) => {
1335 | 	console.log("💰 Creating payments...");
1336 | 	const payments: (typeof payment.$inferSelect)[] = [];
1337 | 
1338 | 	const paymentAppointments = getRandomSubset(appointments, CONFIG.totalPayments);
1339 | 
1340 | 	for (const appointment of paymentAppointments) {
1341 | 		const patient = patients.find(p => p.id === appointment.patientId);
1342 | 		if (!patient) continue;
1343 | 
1344 | 		const totalAmount = faker.number.int({ min: 50, max: 500 });
1345 | 		const amountPaid = faker.datatype.boolean(0.8) ? totalAmount : faker.number.int({ min: 0, max: totalAmount });
1346 | 
1347 | 		const status =
1348 | 			amountPaid >= totalAmount
1349 | 				? PaymentStatus.PAID
1350 | 				: amountPaid > 0
1351 | 					? PaymentStatus.PARTIAL
1352 | 					: PaymentStatus.UNPAID;
1353 | 
1354 | 		const paymentData = {
1355 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
1356 | 			clinicId: appointment.clinicId,
1357 | 			patientId: appointment.patientId,
1358 | 			appointmentId: appointment.id,
1359 | 			billDate: appointment.appointmentDate,
1360 | 			paymentDate:
1361 | 				status === PaymentStatus.PAID
1362 | 					? faker.date.between({
1363 | 							from:
1364 | 								appointment.appointmentDate > new Date()
1365 | 									? appointment.createdAt
1366 | 									: appointment.appointmentDate,
1367 | 							to: new Date()
1368 | 						})
1369 | 					: null,
1370 | 			discount: faker.datatype.boolean(0.2) ? faker.number.int({ min: 5, max: 50 }) : null,
1371 | 			totalAmount,
1372 | 			amountPaid,
1373 | 			amount: totalAmount,
1374 | 			status: status as PaymentStatus,
1375 | 			insurance: faker.datatype.boolean(0.3) ? faker.company.name() : null,
1376 | 			insuranceId: faker.datatype.boolean(0.2) ? faker.string.alphanumeric(10) : null,
1377 | 			serviceDate: appointment.appointmentDate,
1378 | 			dueDate: faker.date.future({ years: 0.5 }),
1379 | 			paidDate:
1380 | 				status === PaymentStatus.PAID
1381 | 					? faker.date.between({
1382 | 							from:
1383 | 								appointment.appointmentDate > new Date()
1384 | 									? appointment.createdAt
1385 | 									: appointment.appointmentDate,
1386 | 							to: new Date()
1387 | 						})
1388 | 					: null,
1389 | 			notes: faker.datatype.boolean(0.3) ? faker.lorem.sentence() : null,
1390 | 			paymentMethod: getRandomEnumValue(PaymentMethod),
1391 | 			receiptNumber: faker.number.int({ min: 1000, max: 9999 }),
1392 | 			isDeleted: false,
1393 | 			deletedAt: null,
1394 | 			billId: null,
1395 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
1396 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
1397 | 		};
1398 | 
1399 | 		await db.insert(payment).values(paymentData);
1400 | 		payments.push(paymentData);
1401 | 
1402 | 		// Create patient bills
1403 | 		if (faker.datatype.boolean(0.6)) {
1404 | 			await createPatientBill(db, paymentData, services);
1405 | 		}
1406 | 	}
1407 | 
1408 | 	return payments;
1409 | };

1721 | 	for (const vaccine of vaccineData) {
1722 | 		const schedule = {
1723 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
1724 | 			vaccineName: vaccine.name,
1725 | 			recommendedAge: vaccine.recommendedAge,
1726 | 			dosesRequired: vaccine.dosesRequired,
1727 | 			minimumInterval: faker.number.int({ min: 30, max: 180 }),
1728 | 			isMandatory: faker.datatype.boolean(0.8),
1729 | 			ageInDaysMin: vaccine.ageInDaysMin,
1730 | 			ageInDaysMax: vaccine.ageInDaysMax,
1731 | 			description: faker.lorem.sentence(),
1732 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
1733 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
1734 | 		};
1735 | 
1736 | 		try {
1737 | 			await db.insert(vaccineSchedule).values(schedule);
1738 | 			schedules.push(schedule);
1739 | 		} catch (error) {
1740 | 			// Ignore duplicate key errors for upsert-like behavior
1741 | 			if (!(error instanceof Error && error.message.includes("UNIQUE constraint failed"))) {
1742 | 				throw error;
1743 | 			}
1744 | 		}
1745 | 	}
1746 | 
1747 | 	return schedules;
1748 | };
1749 | 
1750 | // Create guardians
1751 | const createGuardians = async (
1752 | 	db: DB,
1753 | 	patients: (typeof patient.$inferSelect)[],
1754 | 	users: (typeof user.$inferSelect)[]
1755 | ) => {
1756 | 	console.log("👨‍👩‍👧 Creating guardians...");
1757 | 	const guardians = [];
1758 | 
1759 | 	for (const patient of patients) {
1760 | 		if (faker.datatype.boolean(0.7)) {
1761 | 			const guardianUser = faker.helpers.arrayElement(
1762 | 				users.filter(u => u.role !== "doctor" && u.role !== "staff")
1763 | 			);
1764 | 
1765 | 			const newGuardian = {
1766 | 				id: faker.string.uuid(),
1767 | 				patientId: patient.id,
1768 | 				userId: guardianUser.id,
1769 | 				relation: faker.helpers.arrayElement(["Parent", "Guardian", "Spouse", "Sibling"]),
1770 | 				isPrimary: true,
1771 | 				phone: faker.phone.number(),
1772 | 				email: guardianUser.email
1773 | 			};
1774 | 
1775 | 			await db.insert(guardian).values(newGuardian);
1776 | 			guardians.push(newGuardian);
1777 | 		}
1778 | 	}
1779 | 
1780 | 	return guardians;
1781 | };
1782 | 
1783 | // Create sample files
1784 | const createSampleFiles = async (db: DB, users: (typeof user.$inferSelect)[]) => {
1785 | 	console.log("📁 Creating sample files...");
1786 | 	for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
1787 | 		const randomUser = faker.helpers.arrayElement(users);
1788 | 
1789 | 		await db.insert(file).values({
1790 | 			id: faker.string.uuid(),
1791 | 			slug: faker.string.alphanumeric(10),
1792 | 			userId: randomUser.id,
1793 | 			filename: faker.system.fileName(),
1794 | 			searchText: faker.lorem.words(3),
1795 | 			size: faker.number.int({ min: 1000, max: 1000000 }),
1796 | 			mimeType: faker.system.mimeType(),
1797 | 			folderId: null,
1798 | 			createdAt: new Date(),
1799 | 			updatedAt: new Date()
1800 | 		});
1801 | 	}
1802 | };
1803 | 
1804 | // Main seed function
1805 | export async function runSeed(db: DB) {
1806 | 	try {
1807 | 		console.log("🌱 Starting comprehensive seed process...");
1808 | 
1809 | 		// Clear existing data
1810 | 		await clearAllData(db);
1811 | 
1812 | 		// Create basic entities
1813 | 		const clinicsData = await createClinics(db);
1814 | 		const users = await createUsers(db);
1815 | 		await associateUsersWithClinics(db, users, clinicsData);
1816 | 
1817 | 		const doctors = await createDoctors(db, users, clinicsData);
1818 | 		const staffData = await createStaff(db, users, clinicsData);
1819 | 		const patients = await createPatients(db, users, clinicsData);
1820 | 		const services = await createServices(db, clinicsData);
1821 | 
1822 | 		// Create appointments and related data
1823 | 		const appointments = await createAppointments(db, patients, doctors, services);
1824 | 		const medicalRecords = await createMedicalRecords(db, patients, appointments, services);
1825 | 
1826 | 		// Create additional data
1827 | 		const { drugs, prescriptions } = await createDrugsAndPrescriptions(db, medicalRecords, patients, doctors);
1828 | 		const payments = await createPayments(db, appointments, patients, services);
1829 | 		const immunizations = await createImmunizations(db, medicalRecords, staffData);
1830 | 		const feedingLogs = await createFeedingLogs(db, patients);
1831 | 		const developmentalCheckResults = await createDevelopmentalChecks(db, patients);
1832 | 		await createRatings(db, doctors, patients);
1833 | 		const whoStandards = await createWHOGrowthStandards(db);
1834 | 		const vaccineSchedules = await createVaccineSchedules(db);
1835 | 		const guardians = await createGuardians(db, patients, users);
1836 | 		await createSampleFiles(db, users);
1837 | 
1838 | 		console.log("\n🎉 Seed completed successfully!");
1839 | 		console.log("📊 Summary of created data:");
1840 | 		console.log(`🏥 Clinics: ${clinicsData.length}`);
1841 | 		console.log(`👥 Users: ${users.length}`);
1842 | 		console.log(`👨‍⚕️ Doctors: ${doctors.length}`);
1843 | 		console.log(`👨‍💼 Staff: ${staffData.length}`);
1844 | 		console.log(`👤 Patients: ${patients.length}`);
1845 | 		console.log(`🩺 Services: ${services.length}`);
1846 | 		console.log(`📅 Appointments: ${appointments.length}`);
1847 | 		console.log(`📋 Medical Records: ${medicalRecords.length}`);
1848 | 		console.log(`💊 Drugs: ${drugs.length}`);
1849 | 		console.log(`💊 Prescriptions: ${prescriptions.length}`);
1850 | 		console.log(`💰 Payments: ${payments.length}`);
1851 | 		console.log(`💉 Immunizations: ${immunizations.length}`);
1852 | 		console.log(`🍼 Feeding Logs: ${feedingLogs.length}`);
1853 | 		console.log(`📊 Developmental Checks: ${developmentalCheckResults.length}`);
1854 | 		console.log("⭐ Ratings: created for doctors");
1855 | 		console.log(`📏 WHO Growth Standards: ${whoStandards.length}`);
1856 | 		console.log(`📋 Vaccine Schedules: ${vaccineSchedules.length}`);
1857 | 		console.log(`👨‍👩‍👧 Guardians: ${guardians.length}`);
1858 | 	} catch (error) {
1859 | 		console.error("❌ Error during seed:", error);
1860 | 		throw error;
1861 | 	}
1862 | }
```
