`seed/wfa.ts`:

```ts
   1 | // scripts/seed-who-growth-data.ts
   2 | 
   3 | import { randomUUID } from "node:crypto";
   4 | import fs from "node:fs";
   5 | import path from "node:path";
   6 | 
   7 | import { db } from "../";
   8 | import { whoGrowthStandard } from "../schema";
   9 | import { Gender } from "../seed/seed";
  10 | 
  11 | type WHODayData = {
  12 | 	Day: string;
  13 | 	L: string;
  14 | 	M: string;
  15 | 	S: string;
  16 | 	SD4neg: string;
  17 | 	SD3neg: string;
  18 | 	SD2neg: string;
  19 | 	SD1neg: string;
  20 | 	SD0: string;
  21 | 	SD1: string;
  22 | 	SD2: string;
  23 | 	SD3: string;
  24 | 	SD4: string;
  25 | };
  26 | 
  27 | type WHOData = {
  28 | 	wfa: {
  29 | 		boys: WHODayData[];
  30 | 		girls: WHODayData[];
  31 | 	};
  32 | };
  33 | 
  34 | export default async function seedWHOGrowthData() {
  35 | 	console.log("🌱 Seeding WHO growth data...");
  36 | 
  37 | 	// 1️⃣ Read JSON
  38 | 	const dataPath = path.join(process.cwd(), "data", "wfa.json");
  39 | 	const rawData = fs.readFileSync(dataPath, "utf-8");
  40 | 	const whoData = JSON.parse(rawData) as WHOData;
  41 | 
  42 | 	// 2️⃣ Clear existing data (fastest & safest)
  43 | 	console.log("🗑️ Clearing existing WHO growth data...");
  44 | 	await db.delete(whoGrowthStandard).execute();
  45 | 
  46 | 	const records: (typeof whoGrowthStandard.$inferInsert)[] = [];
  47 | 
  48 | 	// 3️⃣ Boys
  49 | 	for (const dayData of whoData.wfa.boys) {
  50 | 		const ageDays = Number.parseInt(dayData.Day, 10);
  51 | 
  52 | 		records.push({
  53 | 			id: randomUUID(),
  54 | 			ageDays,
  55 | 			ageInMonths: Math.floor(ageDays / 30.4375),
  56 | 			gender: Gender.MALE,
  57 | 			measurementType: "WEIGHT",
  58 | 			lValue: Number(dayData.L),
  59 | 			mValue: Number(dayData.M),
  60 | 			sValue: Number(dayData.S),
  61 | 			sd0: Number(dayData.SD0),
  62 | 			sd1neg: Number(dayData.SD1neg),
  63 | 			sd1pos: Number(dayData.SD1),
  64 | 			sd2neg: Number(dayData.SD2neg),
  65 | 			sd2pos: Number(dayData.SD2),
  66 | 			sd3neg: Number(dayData.SD3neg),
  67 | 			sd3pos: Number(dayData.SD3),
  68 | 			sd4neg: Number(dayData.SD4neg),
  69 | 			sd4pos: Number(dayData.SD4)
  70 | 		});
  71 | 	}
  72 | 
  73 | 	// 4️⃣ Girls
  74 | 	for (const dayData of whoData.wfa.girls) {
  75 | 		const ageDays = Number.parseInt(dayData.Day, 10);
  76 | 
  77 | 		records.push({
  78 | 			id: randomUUID(),
  79 | 			ageDays,
  80 | 			ageInMonths: Math.floor(ageDays / 30.4375),
  81 | 			gender: Gender.FEMALE,
  82 | 			measurementType: "WEIGHT",
  83 | 			lValue: Number(dayData.L),
  84 | 			mValue: Number(dayData.M),
  85 | 			sValue: Number(dayData.S),
  86 | 			sd0: Number(dayData.SD0),
  87 | 			sd1neg: Number(dayData.SD1neg),
  88 | 			sd1pos: Number(dayData.SD1),
  89 | 			sd2neg: Number(dayData.SD2neg),
  90 | 			sd2pos: Number(dayData.SD2),
  91 | 			sd3neg: Number(dayData.SD3neg),
  92 | 			sd3pos: Number(dayData.SD3),
  93 | 			sd4neg: Number(dayData.SD4neg),
  94 | 			sd4pos: Number(dayData.SD4)
  95 | 		});
  96 | 	}
  97 | 
  98 | 	// 5️⃣ Batched insert (SQLite-safe)
  99 | 	const BATCH_SIZE = 1000;
 100 | 	let inserted = 0;
 101 | 
 102 | 	for (let i = 0; i < records.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
 103 | 		const batch = records.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE);
 104 | 
 105 | 		await db.insert(whoGrowthStandard).values(batch).execute();
 106 | 
 107 | 		inserted += batch.length;
 108 | 		console.log(`  ✅ Inserted ${batch.length} records`);
 109 | 	}
 110 | 
 111 | 	console.log(`🎉 Seeded ${inserted} WHO WFA records`);
 112 | }

```

   1 | import type { InferSelectModel } from "drizzle-orm";

  11 | });

 309 | // Time validation regex
 310 | const TIME_REGEX = /^([0-1]?[0-9]|2[0-3]):[0-5][0-9]$/;
 311 | 
 312 | // User Quota Schema with enhanced validation
 313 | export const UserQuotaEnhancedCreateSchema = createInsertSchema(userQuota, {
 314 | 	userId: z.string().min(1, "User ID is required"),
 315 | 	quota: z.number().int().min(0, "Quota must be non-negative"),
 316 | 	usedQuota: z.number().int().min(0, "Used quota must be non-negative"),
 317 | 	fileCount: z.number().int().min(0, "File count must be non-negative"),
 318 | 	fileCountQuota: z.number().int().min(0, "File count quota must be non-negative"),
 319 | 	inviteCount: z.number().int().min(0, "Invite count must be non-negative"),
 320 | 	inviteQuota: z.number().int().min(0, "Invite quota must be non-negative")
 321 | }).omit({ updatedAt: true });
 322 | 
 323 | export const UserQuotaEnhancedUpdateSchema = UserQuotaEnhancedCreateSchema.safeExtend({
 324 | 	userId: z.string().min(1, "User ID is required")
 325 | });
 326 | 
 327 | // Folder Schema with enhanced validation
 328 | export const FolderEnhancedCreateSchema = createInsertSchema(folder)
 329 | 	.omit({
 330 | 		createdAt: true,
 331 | 		updatedAt: true,
 332 | 		id: true,
 333 | 		userId: true,
 334 | 		name: true,
 335 | 		parentId: true
 336 | 	})
 337 | 	.extend({
 338 | 		id: z.string().min(1, "Folder ID is required"),
 339 | 		userId: z.string().min(1, "User ID is required"),
 340 | 		name: z.string().min(1, "Folder name is required").max(255, "Folder name too long"),
 341 | 		parentId: z.string().nullable().optional()
 342 | 	});
 343 |

 345 | 	id: z.string().min(1, "Folder ID is required")
 346 | });

 406 | // Doctor Schema with enhanced validation
 407 | export const DoctorEnhancedCreateSchema = createInsertSchema(doctor)
 408 | 	.omit({
 409 | 		createdAt: true,
 410 | 		updatedAt: true,
 411 | 		id: true,
 412 | 		name: true,
 413 | 		specialty: true,
 414 | 		email: true,
 415 | 		userId: true,
 416 | 		clinicId: true,
 417 | 		licenseNumber: true,
 418 | 		phone: true,
 419 | 		address: true,
 420 | 		department: true,
 421 | 		img: true,
 422 | 		colorCode: true,
 423 | 		availabilityStatus: true,
 424 | 		availableFromWeekDay: true,
 425 | 		availableToWeekDay: true,
 426 | 		isActive: true,
 427 | 		status: true,
 428 | 		availableFromTime: true,
 429 | 		availableToTime: true,
 430 | 		type: true,
 431 | 		appointmentPrice: true,
 432 | 		role: true,
 433 | 		rating: true,
 434 | 		deletedAt: true,
 435 | 		isDeleted: true
 436 | 	})
 437 | 	.extend({
 438 | 		id: z.string().min(1, "Doctor ID is required"),
 439 | 		email: z.email("Invalid email format").nullable().optional(),
 440 | 		name: z.string().min(1, "Doctor name is required"),
 441 | 		userId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
 442 | 		clinicId: z.string().nullable().optional(),
 443 | 		specialty: z.string().min(1, "Specialty is required"),
 444 | 		licenseNumber: z.string().nullable().optional(),
 445 | 		phone: z.string().nullable().optional(),
 446 | 		address: z.string().nullable().optional(),
 447 | 		department: z.string().nullable().optional(),
 448 | 		img: z.string().url("Invalid image URL").nullable().optional(),
 449 | 		colorCode: z
 450 | 			.string()
 451 | 			.regex(/^#[0-9A-F]{6}$/i, "Invalid color code")
 452 | 			.nullable()
 453 | 			.optional(),
 454 | 		availabilityStatus: z.enum(["AVAILABLE", "UNAVAILABLE", "ON_LEAVE"]).nullable().optional(),
 455 | 		availableFromWeekDay: z
 456 | 			.enum(["MONDAY", "TUESDAY", "WEDNESDAY", "THURSDAY", "FRIDAY", "SATURDAY", "SUNDAY"])
 457 | 			.nullable()
 458 | 			.optional(),
 459 | 		availableToWeekDay: z
 460 | 			.enum(["MONDAY", "TUESDAY", "WEDNESDAY", "THURSDAY", "FRIDAY", "SATURDAY", "SUNDAY"])
 461 | 			.nullable()
 462 | 			.optional(),
 463 | 		isActive: z.boolean().nullable().optional(),
 464 | 		status: z
 465 | 			.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "PENDING", "SUSPENDED", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED", "EXPIRED", "ON_HOLD"])
 466 | 			.nullable()
 467 | 			.optional(),
 468 | 		availableFromTime: z.string().regex(TIME_REGEX, "Invalid time format").nullable().optional(),
 469 | 		availableToTime: z.string().regex(TIME_REGEX, "Invalid time format").nullable().optional(),
 470 | 		type: z.enum(["FULL", "PART_TIME", "CONSULTANT", "VISITING"]).default("FULL"),
 471 | 		appointmentPrice: z.number().int().min(0, "Price must be non-negative").nullable().optional(),
 472 | 		role: z.enum(["admin", "doctor", "staff", "patient"]).nullable().optional(),
 473 | 		rating: z.number().int().min(0).max(5, "Rating must be between 0 and 5").nullable().optional(),
 474 | 		deletedAt: z.date().nullable().optional(),
 475 | 		isDeleted: z.boolean().default(false)
 476 | 	});
 477 | 
 478 | export const DoctorEnhancedUpdateSchema = DoctorEnhancedCreateSchema.safeExtend({
 479 | 	id: z.string().min(1, "Doctor ID is required")
 480 | });

 482 | // Working Day Schema with enhanced validation
 483 | const WorkingDayBaseSchema = createInsertSchema(workingDay)
 484 | 	.omit({
 485 | 		createdAt: true,
 486 | 		updatedAt: true,
 487 | 		id: true,
 488 | 		doctorId: true,
 489 | 		day: true,
 490 | 		startTime: true,
 491 | 		endTime: true
 492 | 	})
 493 | 	.extend({
 494 | 		id: z.string().min(1, "Working day ID is required"),
 495 | 		doctorId: z.string().min(1, "Doctor ID is required"),
 496 | 		day: z.enum(["MONDAY", "TUESDAY", "WEDNESDAY", "THURSDAY", "FRIDAY", "SATURDAY", "SUNDAY"]),
 497 | 		startTime: z.string().regex(TIME_REGEX, "Invalid start time format"),
 498 | 		endTime: z.string().regex(TIME_REGEX, "Invalid end time format")
 499 | 	});
 500 | 
 501 | export const WorkingDayEnhancedCreateSchema = WorkingDayBaseSchema.refine(data => data.startTime < data.endTime, {
 502 | 	message: "Start time must be before end time",
 503 | 	path: ["endTime"]
 504 | });
 505 | 
 506 | export const WorkingDayEnhancedUpdateSchema = WorkingDayEnhancedCreateSchema.safeExtend({
 507 | 	id: z.string().min(1, "Working day ID is required")
 508 | });

 590 | export const BulkPatientUpdateSchema = z.object({
 591 | 	patientIds: z.array(z.string().min(1)).min(1, "At least one patient ID is required"),
 592 | 	updates: z
 593 | 		.object({
 594 | 			status: z
 595 | 				.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "PENDING", "SUSPENDED", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED", "EXPIRED", "ON_HOLD"])
 596 | 				.optional(),
 597 | 			isActive: z.boolean().optional(),
 598 | 			updatedById: z.string().optional()
 599 | 		})
 600 | 		.refine(data => Object.keys(data).length > 0, {
 601 | 			message: "At least one field must be updated"
 602 | 		})
 603 | });
 604 | 
 605 | export const BulkAppointmentUpdateSchema = z.object({
 606 | 	appointmentIds: z.array(z.string().min(1)).min(1, "At least one appointment ID is required"),
 607 | 	updates: z
 608 | 		.object({
 609 | 			status: z.enum(["PENDING", "CONFIRMED", "COMPLETED", "CANCELLED", "NO_SHOW"]).optional(),
 610 | 			doctorId: z.string().optional(),
 611 | 			appointmentDate: z.date().optional()
 612 | 		})
 613 | 		.refine(data => Object.keys(data).length > 0, {
 614 | 			message: "At least one field must be updated"
 615 | 		})
 616 | });
 617 |

 624 | 	)

 771 | export type AdherenceItem = DbPrescribedItem & {
 772 | 	prescription?: DbPrescription | null;
 773 | 	dispenses?: {
 774 | 		quantityDispensed: number;
 775 | 	}[];
 776 | 	dosageValue: number | null;
 777 | 	frequency: string;
 778 | };
 779 | 
 780 | // Helper functions
 781 | export function calculateAdherenceMetrics(prescribedItems: AdherenceItem[]) {
 782 | 	let totalAdherence = 0;
 783 | 	let count = 0;
 784 | 
 785 | 	for (const item of prescribedItems) {
 786 | 		const expectedDoses = calculateExpectedDoses(
 787 | 			item,
 788 | 			item.prescription?.issuedDate ?? new Date(),
 789 | 			item.prescription?.validUntil ?? new Date()
 790 | 		);
 791 | 		const dispensedDoses =
 792 | 			item.dispenses?.reduce(
 793 | 				(sum: number, dispense: { quantityDispensed: number }) =>
 794 | 					sum + dispense.quantityDispensed / (item.dosageValue || 1),
 795 | 				0
 796 | 			) ?? 0;
 797 | 
 798 | 		const adherence = expectedDoses > 0 ? (dispensedDoses / expectedDoses) * 100 : 0;
 799 | 		totalAdherence += adherence;
 800 | 		count++;
 801 | 	}
 802 | 
 803 | 	return {
 804 | 		overallAdherence: count > 0 ? totalAdherence / count : 0,
 805 | 		status: getAdherenceStatus(totalAdherence / count)
 806 | 	};
 807 | }
 808 | 
 809 | function getAdherenceStatus(percentage: number): "GOOD" | "FAIR" | "POOR" {
 810 | 	if (percentage >= 80) return "GOOD";
 811 | 	if (percentage >= 50) return "FAIR";
 812 | 	return "POOR";
 813 | }
 814 | 
 815 | export function calculateExpectedDoses(item: AdherenceItem, startDate: Date, endDate: Date) {
 816 | 	const days = Math.ceil((endDate.getTime() - startDate.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
 817 | 	const frequencyPerDay = parseFrequency(item.frequency);
 818 | 	return days * frequencyPerDay * (item.dosageValue || 1);
 819 | }
 820 | export type PrescriptionWithItems = DbPrescription & {
 821 | 	prescribedItems: (DbPrescribedItem & {
 822 | 		drug?: DbDrug | null;
 823 | 	})[];
 824 | };
 825 | 
 826 | function parseFrequency(frequency: string): number {
 827 | 	const f = frequency.toUpperCase();
 828 | 	if (f.includes("QD") || f.includes("ONCE")) return 1;
 829 | 	if (f.includes("BID") || f.includes("TWICE")) return 2;
 830 | 	if (f.includes("TID") || f.includes("THREE")) return 3;
 831 | 	if (f.includes("QID") || f.includes("FOUR")) return 4;
 832 | 	if (f.includes("QHS")) return 1;
 833 | 	return 1;
 834 | }

`zod/filter.schema.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import { z } from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | export const filterOperators = [
   4 | 	"eq",
   5 | 	"ne",
   6 | 	"lt",
   7 | 	"lte",
   8 | 	"gt",
   9 | 	"gte",
  10 | 	"ilike",
  11 | 	"notIlike",
  12 | 	"isEmpty",
  13 | 	"isNotEmpty",
  14 | 	"inArray",
  15 | 	"notInArray",
  16 | 	"between"
  17 | ] as const;
  18 | 
  19 | export const filterVariants = ["text", "number", "date", "select", "multiSelect", "boolean"] as const;
  20 | 
  21 | export const filterSchema = z.object({
  22 | 	id: z.string(),
  23 | 	value: z.union([z.string(), z.array(z.string())]),
  24 | 	variant: z.enum(filterVariants),
  25 | 	operator: z.enum(filterOperators),
  26 | 	filterId: z.string()
  27 | });
  28 | 
  29 | export type FilterSchema = z.infer<typeof filterSchema>;

`zod/pagination.schema.ts`:

```ts
   1 | import z from "zod";
   2 | 
   3 | import { filterSchema } from "./filter.schema";
   4 | 
   5 | /**
   6 |  * Creates a reusable pagination schema with shared filtering, sorting, and soft-delete fields.
   7 |  * Pass in your resource-specific sortable fields enum to generate a fully typed schema.
   8 |  *
   9 |  * @example
  10 |  * ```ts
  11 |  * const SORTABLE_CLUSTER_FIELDS = ["name", "createdAt", "updatedAt"] as const;
  12 |  *
  13 |  * const getAllClustersSchema = createPaginationSchema(SORTABLE_CLUSTER_FIELDS).extend({
  14 |  *   name: z.string().default(""),
  15 |  * });
  16 |  * ```
  17 |  */
  18 | export function createPaginationSchema<T extends readonly [string, ...Array<string>]>(
  19 | 	sortableFields: T,
  20 | 	defaultSort: { id: T[number]; desc: boolean } = {
  21 | 		id: sortableFields[0],
  22 | 		desc: false
  23 | 	}
  24 | ) {
  25 | 	return z.object({
  26 | 		page: z.number().int().min(1).default(1),
  27 | 		perPage: z.number().int().min(1).max(100).default(10),
  28 | 		sort: z
  29 | 			.array(
  30 | 				z.object({
  31 | 					id: z.enum(sortableFields),
  32 | 					desc: z.boolean()
  33 | 				})
  34 | 			)
  35 | 			.default([defaultSort]),
  36 | 		createdAt: z.array(z.coerce.number()).default([]),
  37 | 		filters: z.array(filterSchema).default([]),
  38 | 		joinOperator: z.enum(["and", "or"]).default("and")
  39 | 	});
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | /**
  43 |  * Creates a reusable cursor-based pagination schema for infinite scrolling.
  44 |  * Pass in your resource-specific sortable fields enum to generate a fully typed schema.
  45 |  *
  46 |  * @example
  47 |  * ```ts
  48 |  * const SORTABLE_CLUSTER_FIELDS = ["name", "createdAt", "updatedAt"] as const;
  49 |  *
  50 |  * const getClustersInfiniteSchema = createCursorPaginationSchema(SORTABLE_CLUSTER_FIELDS).extend({
  51 |  *   name: z.string().default(""),
  52 |  * });
  53 |  * ```
  54 |  */
  55 | export function createCursorPaginationSchema<T extends readonly [string, ...Array<string>]>(
  56 | 	sortableFields: T,
  57 | 	defaultSort: { id: T[number]; desc: boolean } = {
  58 | 		id: sortableFields[0],
  59 | 		desc: false
  60 | 	}
  61 | ) {
  62 | 	return z.object({
  63 | 		cursor: z.string().optional(), // The cursor for the next page (usually an encoded ID or timestamp)
  64 | 		limit: z.number().int().min(1).max(100).default(20),
  65 | 		sort: z
  66 | 			.object({
  67 | 				id: z.enum(sortableFields),
  68 | 				desc: z.boolean()
  69 | 			})
  70 | 			.default(defaultSort),
  71 | 		createdAt: z.array(z.coerce.number()).default([]),
  72 | 		filters: z.array(filterSchema).default([]),
  73 | 		joinOperator: z.enum(["and", "or"]).default("and")
  74 | 	});
  75 | }

```
